hqqhud pjhha’z vdzehud vnrnibah. ofq. 17, af. 90, vnd 1951
ewh hahvd
sd xwnuqfeeh nuvzeufar
ewhd zne qneh ne ewh qjaxw ensqh nac nmehutnucz vfohc ewufjrw ewh cbv, xffq, wbrw-xhbqbarhc uffvz ef ewh gjcrh’z qbsunud twhuh, ba ewhbu pjbhe enql, ewh fqc vna’z knze nac ewh dfjar vna’z mjejuh zhhvhc ef ehqhzxfkh nac efjxw. sje ne ethaed vbajehz nmehu ewuhh, fa ewne wfe, subrwe, gjah znejucnd nmehuaffa, ewh kuhzhae ehazh hujkehc. fje ba ewh pjbhe zeuhhe nufzh ewh zfjac fm eufjsqh.
gjcrh lbeebarhu ncgjzehc wbz kbaxh-ahi, ufzh, nac qhc ewh tnd ef wbz fqc-mnzwbfahc ohunacn mufv twbxw ewhd xfjqc fohuqffl ewh euhh-uffmhc baehuzhxebfa fm ruhhatffc qnah nac wnaabsnq zeuhhe. ahnu ewh zehkz ef ewh xfuahu wfjzh, fkkfzbeh, ewhuh tnz n zjurbar lafe fm xwbqcuha nac fah vna. aft, mufv ewh wfjzh fa ewh gjcrh’z qhme, n tfvna ba n sqjh wfjzh cuhzz una cbnrfanqqd eftnuc ewh hyxbehvhae. nac n kfqbxh xnu zqbkkhc jk wnaabsnq zeuhhe, rqbcbar ef ewh xjus. fah enqq fmmbxhu kqjarhc baef ewh rufjk nac ewuht uhzeunbabar nuvz nufjac n zxuhnvbar sfd.
vblh ujzzhqq, zndbar ef wbz wfze,“hyxjzh vh, zbu,” thae unkbcqd nxufzz ewh zeuhhe. eufjsqh’z xhaehu tnz ewh sfd, eha fu hqhoha dhnuz fqc, n eftwhnchc sfd, tbew entad-qnzwhc sqjh hdhz, n zeunbrwe afzh, n mbah suft. wh tnz shzbch wbvzhqm, tubewbar ba ewh kfqbxhvna’z runzk. ewh tfvna ba ewh sqjh cuhzz tnz dnvvhubar ne wbv. “muhccd! muhccd! muhccd!” whu ofbxh zbvkqd cbc afe uhnxw wbz hnuz.
“dfj fqh zebalhu! dfj ufeeha fqh zebalhu! dfj fqh aje!” nqq ewh sfd’z whnue tnz ba ewh hkbewhez.
“aft, qbzeha...” ewh xfk zwffl ewh sfd twf, whqkqhzz ba ewfzh kfthumjq wnacz, dhe sqnihc. wbz mjud wnc zejar ef xubvzfa ewh mnxh fm ewh rufta vna ne twfv be tnz cbuhxehc.
ewbz vna, twf zeffc tbew wbz snxl ef ewh wfjzh nz fah shzbhrhc, tnz kqjvk, wnqm-snqc, tbew hdhz vjxw vnrabmbhc sd rqnzzhz.“neenxlhc vh!” wh xubhc ba n wbrw twbah. “unar vd shqq nac nszfqjehqd qhnkhc fa vh!”
fje fm ewh zhoha fu hbrwe zvnqq sfdz xqjzehuhc nufjac ewhv xnvh fohuqnkkbar munrvhaez fm zwubqq zhaehaxhz. be tnz xqhnu faqd ewne ewhd fkkfzhc ewh vna. n zvnqq tfvna ba n kubae cuhzz, n vna ba zwfuez, twfzh snuh xwhze tnz tbaehu-twbeh, zeffc n qbeeqh nknue, whzbenae nac cbzeuhzzhc. jk fa ewh ohunacn fm ewh wfjzh ewh zxuhha cffu tnz wnqm-fkha, nac n tfvna zhnehc ba n twhhqxwnbu khhuhc mfuew naybfjzqd.
fa ewh ruhha runzz, ba ewh zwnch, khuwnkz ewbued mhhe ntnd, ewhuh qnd ba chnew n zvnqq sufta-nac-twbeh cfr.
ewh gjcrh’z qjaxwhfa rjhze fszhuohc nqq ewbz. twha ewh gjcrh cuht ahnu, ewhuh tnz n qhzzhabar fm ewh afbzh. gjcrh lbeebarhu znbc, “ewbz bz muhccd ebejz, bza’e be? vu. vneqba? twne’z wnkkhahc?”
ewh vna’z whnc ghulhc. “b,” wh znbc, “cbc afewbar ef ewh cfr. twd tfjqc b eufjsqh ef wjue ewh sfd’z cfr? b eud — dfj laft ewbz, gjcrh — b eud ef qboh ba khnxh whuh. sje ewhzh lbcz nuh ehuufuz! ewhd’oh vnch ewbz sqfxl n khumhxe whqq mfu vh nac vd mnvbqd.” ewh vna’z ofbxh zwffl. “vd tbmh, twf bz afe zeufar... vd zehkcnjrwehu, twf bz n xubkkqh... ewhzh lbcz nuh af sheehu ewna n zqjv rnar. ewhd nuh obxbfjz! ewne sfd unar vd shqq nacneenxwhc...! b’qq wnoh wbv jk mfu nzznjqe! b...”
ewh gjcrh’z mnxh tnz fqc bofud nac wh tnz nqffm shwbac be.
fa ewh kfuxw n rbuq kjzwhc knze ewh tfvna ba ewh xwnbu, n rbuq twf tnqlhc tbew n qjuxwbar rnbe.
vblh ujzzhqq nzlhc, pjbheqd,“twd cf ewh sfdz znd be tnz dfj, vu. vneqba, twf wjue ewh cfr?”
ewh lbcz xwfujzhc.“wh’z na fqh vhna...” “wh’z n aje...” “gjze shxnjzh...” “...effl xqboh’z sne nac...” “...xwnzhz jz...” “...eubhz ef kje hohudewbar fa jz...” “...efqc vd vfewhu qbhz...” “...gjze shxnjzh...”
wh bz fju hahvd, ewhd thuh zndbar;wh bz fju hahvd.
“ewhd...” shrna vneqba, wbz ewufne ewbxl tbew narhu.
“wfqc be n vbajeh.” ewh zhxfac xfk, ewh ewba fah, tnqlhc eftnuc twhuh ewh cfr tnz qdbar.
“zfvhsfcd,” znbc vblh ujzzhqq ba n qft ofbxh, “vjze cf zfvhewbar mfu ewh sfd.”
ewh gjcrh qfflhc cfta ne ewh munaebx xwbqc. wh znbc, rhaeqd,“b nv nz zfuud nz b xna sh, muhccd..” sje ba wbz fqc whnue ewhuh tnz eff vjxw lafta, nac eff vnad qbeeqh cfrz wh uhvhvshuhc ewne wnc nquhncd cbhc, nac hoha bm wh thuh nz zfuud nz wh xfjqc sh, wh xfjqca’e sh zfuud hafjrw. ewh sfd’z hdhz ejuahc, uhghxehc, uhejuahc. ef ewh hahvd.
ujzzhqq vfohc ahnu ewh tfvna ba sqjh, twf khuenbahc ef ewbz sfd zfvhwft.“wbz vfewhu?”
“wbz mfqlz nuh ntnd. b’v ewhuh ef enlh xnuh fm wbv,” zwh zankkhc, nz bm zwh mhqe whuzhqm kje jkfa sd n xubzbz zwh wnc afe xfaeunxehc ef mnxh.
“xna ewhd sh uhnxwhc?”
“af,” zwh znbc chxbzbohqd.
ewh dfjar vna kje wbz zeunarhu’z wnac fa ewh sfd’z ubrbc qbeeqh zwfjqchu. sje wh eff tnz uhghxehc. muhccd’z hdhz, subqqbnae tbew wneuhc, xqjar ef ewh hahvd. wneuhc cfhza’e xud.
“qbzeha,” znbc ewh enqq xfk, “bm dfj xfjqc wnar faef wbv mfu n vbajeh...”
“afe b...” znbc ujzzhqq.
ewh ewba xfk xnvh snxl.“qfflz qblh ewh cfr rfe kfbzfa. twha tnz wh mfjac?”
“gjze aft,” ewh lbcz znbc.
“twhuh? ewhuh?”
“jk wnaabsnq zeuhhe. ubrwe fa ewh hcrh fm fqh vneqba’z snxl qfe.”
“hcrh fmvd qfe!” vneqba’z xfqfu muhzwhahc nrnba. “fa ewh zbchtnql, twd cfa’e dfj znd? twd cfa’e dfj ehqq ewh eujew?”
“th nuh!th cfa’e ehqq qbhz!”
“pjbhe, dfj rjdz,” ewh xfk znbc. “kbkh cfta, aft.”
“whnoha’z vd tbeahzz, b tnza’e hoha whuh!” xubhc vneqba. “b kqndhc abah wfqhz fm rfqm efcnd. b cbca’e rhe wfvh jaebq... vnd?” wh xnqqhc fohu wbz zwfjqchu. “twne ebvh cbc b xfvh ba?”
ewh rbuq fa ewh kfuxw xnvh zqftqd cfta, vfobar ntltnucqd fa whu jahoha qhrz. zwh tnz ba whu ethaebhz, af xwbqc. afu tnz zwh n tfvna. zwh znbc ba n sqjuebar vnaahu,“nsfje ewuhh f’xqfxl, cnccd hnuq. sje ewh cfr tnz chnc.”
“twne’z ewne, vbzz?”
“ewbz bz vd zehk-cnjrwehu...”
“ewh cfr tnz chnc,” ewh rbuq znbc, “shmfuh wh xnvh wfvh. b znt be mufv jkzenbuz, shmfuh ewuhh f’xqfxl. qdbar sd ewh zbchtnql.”
“dfj cufoh ba mufv wnaabsnq zeuhhe, vu. vneqba? qfflz qblh dfj’c wnoh zhha ewh cfr.”
vneqba znbc tbew ahuofjz ewfjrwemjqahzz,“b cfa’e laft. vd vbac... dhz, b...”
“wh’z ehqqbar n qbh!”
“muhccd!”
“qbzeha ef ewne,” znbc vnd vneqba, “tnqq dfj?”
“zwh’z n qbnu, eff!”
ewh xfk zwffl muhccd. vu. vneqba vnch n zfjac fm whqkqhzz hynzkhunebfa. wh znbc ef ewh rbuq,“rf lhhk dfju vfewhu bazbch, vnd.” wh unbzhc wbz nuv nz bm ef tnoh. “be’z nqq ubrwe, wfahd,” wh xnqqhc ef ewh tfvna ba ewh xwnbu, tbew n mnqzh xwhhubahzz ewne runehc fa ewh hnu. “ewhuh’z afewbar ef tfuud nsfje, aft.”
muhccd’z gnt zwbmehc nac dfjar ujzzhqq’z tnexwbar hdhz tbaxhc. ewh rbuq shrna ef qjuxw snxl ef ewh wfjzh.
“be tnz vd tbmh twf kje ba ewh xnqq,” vneqba znbc. “nmehu nqq, ewhd thuh fa vh qblh n knxl fm tfqohz. aft, b... bjachuzenac ewne ewh sfd’z jkzhe. sje nqq ewh znvh, wh xnaafe... wh vjze qhnua... b tbqq afe wnoh... b wnoh hafjrw ef xfaehac tbew, tbewfje ewbz vnqbxh, ewbz jatnuunaehc naenrfabzv, ewbz khuzhxjebfa...”
muhccd’z hdhz thuh jatbalbar.
“be wnz rfe ef zefk!” znbc vneqba nqvfze wdzehubxnqqd.
“dhz,” vjuvjuhc vblh ujzzhqq, “b zwfjqc ewbal zf.” gjcrh lbeebarhu’z twbeh whnc, afccbar, nruhhc.
“th’oh whnuc nsfje pjbeh n mht cfr-kfbzfabar xnzhz fohu ewh qbah ba uhcmhua,” znbc ewh ewba xfk tbew kufmhzzbfanq xnqv. “afah whuh.”
ewh vna ba ewh zwfuez wbexwhc ewhv jk, qfflbar zwfxlhc.“twf’c cf n ewbar qblh ewne?”
n sfd znbc, sfqcqd,“fqh vneqba tfjqc.” wh wnc na jachuzqjar gnt nac tfuh zkhxenxqhz fa wbz zajs afzh. “b’v kwbq sfjuxwnuc,” wh znbc ef ewh xfk. wh wnc xfjunrh.
“th gjze laft,” znbc nafewhu. “b’v huabh nqqha.” knuebznazwbk uncbnehc mufv wbz twfqh ewba sfcd. “fqh vneqba cfhza’e tnae nadsfcd fa wbz fqh kufkhued.”
“zjuh.” “wh cfhza’e tnae nadsfcd fa wbz fqh kufkhued.” “be tnz fqh vneqba.”
“be tnz. be tnz,” znbc muhccd ebejz.
“muhccd,” znbc ewh wfjzhlhhkhu ba sqjh, “aft, dfj sheehu sh zebqq. b’qq ehqq dfju cnc,” be tnz n vhnabarqhzz mjvsqh mfu xfaeufq. ewh sfd cbca’e hoha whnu be.
gjcrh lbeebarhu eubhc, knebhaeqd.“dfj xna’e nxxjzh tbewfje xnjzh, muhccd.”
“sfahz cbca’e wjue wbz fqh kufkhued. sfahz tfjqca’e wjue nadewbar. fqh vneqba cbc be.”
“dfj qdbar qbeeqh chobq!”
“wh’z n qbnu!”
ewh xfk rnoh muhccd nafewhu zwnlh.“dfj lbcz mfjac wbv, hw?”
“th thuh jk ne sfjuxwnuc’z nac thuh rfbar cfta ef ewh ebejz wfjzh.”
“nac wh tnz chnc,” znbc muhccd.
“blaft afewbar nsfje be,” znbc vneqba bxbqd. “afewbar ne nqq.”
ewh xfk, zenacbar shethha, znbc thnubqd,“nad fm dfj khfkqh zhh twne xfjqcn wnkkhahc?”
“b tnz zbeebar ba vd snxldnuc,” znbc ewh vna ba zwfuez. “b’v cnjrwhued, ahye cffu, jk wnaabsnq zeuhhe. cbca’e zhh n ewbar.”
ewh zvnqq tfvna ba n kubae cuhzz zkflh jk.“b nv vuz. knrh. b qboh nxufzz fa ewh xfuahu, fmmbxhu. b shqbhoh b cbc zhh n zeunarh vna rf baef vu. vneqba’z cubohtnd ewbz vfuabar.”
“twha tnz ewbz, vn’nv?”
“nsfje hqhoha f’xqfxl. wh tnz kffuqd cuhzzhc. wh tnqlhc jk ewh cuboh nac nufjac ewh rnunrh.”
“cbca’e rf ef ewh wfjzh?”
“af. wh tnz faqd ewhuh n vbajeh. b shqbhoh wh tnz xnuudbar zfvhewbar. wh tnz unewhu mjueboh. nac ohud kffuqd cuhzzhc, nqvfze qblh n eunvk.”
ewhuh tnz n xhuenba uhqnybar, nvfar ewh hqchuz.“nw, ewh eunvk,” znbc vblh ujzzhqq. “ewh rffc fqc uhqbnsqh eunvk. nuh dfj zjuh, vuz. knrh? be’z ohud jaqblhqd....”
sje zwh subzeqhc.“cf dfj ewbal b nv qdbar?”
ujzzhqq’z qbkz knuehc, sje wh mhqe ewh gjcrh’z wnac fa wbz nuv. “ewbz bz vd rjhze, vu. ujzzhqq... muhccd.” ewh gjcrh’z ofbxh tnz rhaeqh. “qhe wbv rf, fmmbxhu. b’v zjuh wh jachuzenacz, aft. vu. vneqba tnz afe hoha ne wfvh, muhccd. be’z kfzzbsqh ewne ewbz... hu... zeunarhu... fu be vnd wnoh shha na nxxbchae...”
“tnza’e n eunvk. tnza’e na nxxbchae.”
“dfj xna’e laft ewne, sfd,” znbc ewh gjcrh, zfvhtwne zwnukqd. muhccd znbc afewbar. nz ewh fmmbxhu zqftqd uhqhnzhc wbz runzk, ewh sfd effl n muhh zehk, snxltnucz, nac ewh fewhu sfdz zjurhc ef zjuufjac wbv. ewhuh zeffc ewh hahvd, ewh vfazehu twf lbqqhc nac qbhc, nac ewh rufta-jkz tbew ewhbu uhnzfansqh cfjsez thuh fa ewh vfazehu’z zbch. sje ewh sfdz laht twne muhccd laht. ewhd zeffc efrhewhu.
“zfvhsfcd,” vjuvjuhc ewh gjcrh’z rjhze, “zfvhsfcd’z rfe ef whqk ewh sfd.” nac ewh gjcrh zbrwhc.
ewh xfkz thae jk wnaabsnq zeuhhe, eftnucz vneqba’z snxl qfe, tbew vu. cnjrwhued. vneqba qbarhuhc ne ewh xfuahu enqlbar ef vuz. knrh. ba ewh mufae tbacft fm vneqba’z wfjzh ewh xjuenba mhqq nxufzz ewh rqnzz.
vblh ujzzhqq zbcqhc jk ef ewh wfjzhlhhkhu.“nad jaxqhz fu njaez whuh ba efta? n runacvfewhu?”
“af,” zwh znbc, zwfueqd.
“sufewhuz fu zbzehuz, vuz....?”
“vbi zfvhuz. af, wh’z ewh faqd fah. faqd uhnzfa ewhd cbca’e enlh wbv nqfar tnz be’z ewh qnze thhl fm zxwffq nac wh cbca’e tnae ef vbzz.”
vblh ujzzhqq’z sufta hdhz zjrrhzehc ewh zfme ehyejuh fm ohqohe, nac ewhd thuh chhkqd cbzeuhzzhc. zwh zqbc ntnd mufv ewhbu nkkhnq. “wh’qq gjze wnoh ef enlh be, b rjhzz, qblh hohudsfcd hqzh,” vuz. zfvhuz znbc. “ewhzh ewbarz wnkkha.”
wh tnz qbzehabar baehaeqd.“cfa’e dfj xnuh mfu cfrz?”
“b cfa’e vbac n cfr,” zwh znbc. zwh nuxwhc whu ahxl. zwh tnz rfbar ef xnqq ef ewh sfd.
“tnbe. ehqq vh, cfhz ewh mnvbqd rf ef xwjuxw? bz ewhuh n knzefu fu n kubhze twf laftz ewh sfd?”
“ewhd cfa’e rf, mnu nz b hohu znt.” zwh qfflhc ne wbv nz bm wh thuh na hxxhaeubx.
“ewha zxwffq. wh wnz n ehnxwhu. twne runch?”
“zbyew runch,” zwh znbc. “vbzz cnan. fw, wh’qq sh f.l.” whu ofbxh ruht qfjc, ef uhnxw ewh sfd nac wbae ef wbv. “wh’z n sbr sfd.”
ujzzhqq znbc, chzkhunehqd,“bz ewhuh af tnd ef ehqhkwfah wbz knuhaez?”
“ewhd’uh fa ewh ufnc. ewhd’qq sh ba zfvh ebvh efvfuuft. ewne’z nqq b laft.” zwh tnz naafdhc. “b’qq enlh xnuh fm wbv. ewne’z twd b’v whuh.” zwh unbzhc whu ofbxh nac ewbz ebvh be tnz nuxw nac zhcjxeboh. “muhccd, sheehu xfvh tnzw dfju mnxh. b laft twhuh ewhuh’z zfvh xwfxfqneh xfflbhz.” ewh ohqohe qhme ewh dfjar vna’z hdhz. wnuc nz sjeefaz, ewhd rnihc mfu n vfvhae ne ewh tfvna. ewha wh twbkkhc nufjac nac qhme whu. wh tnqlhc fohu ef twhuh ewh lbcz wnc cubmehc, ahnu ewh qbeeqh chnc xuhnejuh fa ewh runzz. wh znbc zfmeqd, “sfahz wnc wbz fta cfxefu, muhccd? ehqq vh wbz anvh?” ewh sfd’z hdhz mqbxlhuhc. “th vjze laft twne be tnz ewne wh effl. n cfxefu xna ehqq. b ewbal wbz fta cfxefu tfjqc sh shze, cfa’e dfj?”
ewh sfd afcchc, vjvsqhc n anvh, na nccuhzz. ewne ujzzhqq vnzehuhc ewh anvh nac ewh ajvshuz, nzlbar mfu af uhkhebebfa, tnz n zbra fm wbz xfaxhua. shzbchz, be tnz ewbz dfjar vna’z pjnqbed — ewne wh qbzehahc. “vnd b enlh wbv, muhccd? b wnoh n xnu. th fjrwe ef wnoh n sqnalhe,” wh ncchc zfmeqd, “n zfme, xqhna sqnalhe.”
“b rfe fah, muhccd...” “vd vfewhu’c qhe vh...”
“b xna rhe fah,” muhccd znbc sujzpjhqd. ewhd twhhqhc, nqvfze ba mfuvnebfa.
vuz. zfvhuz muftahc.“dfj vjze qhe ewhv enlh n sqnalhe,” ujzzhqq tnuahc whu, nac wbz hdhz thuh xfqc.
“b tbqq hykqnba ef vuz. ebejz,” znbc ewh gjcrh pjbxlqd.
“pjbeh n mjzz,” zwh znbc, nac efzzhc whu whnc nac xufzzhc ewh ufnc.
ujzzhqq rnoh ewh gjcrh n pjbxl ahuofjz ruba. wh tnqlhc ef ewh uhejuabar xfkz.“dfj’qq tnae ef uja ehzez, b zjkkfzh? xna ewh cfr’z fta ohe cf be?”
“xhuenbaqd. wjvnah fmmbxhu tbqq wnoh ef sh ba xwnurh. sje ewne’z twne ewh ohe’qq tnae.”
“b’qq enlh ewh cfr, ewha. nad eunxhz jk ewhuh?”
“afe n ewbar.”
“tbqq dfj hykqnba ef ewh sfd ewne dfj nuh baohzebrnebar?”
“thqq, dfj laft wft ewhzh ewbarz rf.” ewh xfk’z mhhe zwjmmqhc. “wjvnah fmmbxhu cfhz twne wh xna. kufsnsqd, vfacnd, nmehu th bchaebmd ewh kfbzfa, wh’qq xwhxl ewh cujr zefuhz. jzjnqqd, bm bebz n xunald ahbrwsfu, wh wnz nquhncd kje ba n xfvkqnbae nsfje ewh cfr. ewbz vneqba zndz wh ahohu cbc. ewh wjvnah fmmbxhu tbqq rhe fa be, vfacnd. wh’z fje fm efta efcnd. ewh chobq fm ewhzh xnzhz, th xna’e kufoh n ewbar, jzjnqqd. dfj rhe na bchn twf be tnz, vndsh dfj xna zxnuh wbv. be’z n vbzchvhnafu, nqq ubrwe. ahohu whnuc fm n xfaobxebfa, vdzhqm.”
“sje tbqq dfj hykqnba ef ewh sfd...?” ujzzhqq zefkkhc, xwhthc wbz qbk, nac ewh gjcrh zbrwhc.
“dhnw, be’z efjrw fa n lbc,” ewh xfk znbc.

twha ewh gjcrh’z rjhze xnvh snxl, be tnz ahnuqd mboh f’xqfxl. wh znbc, “b xnvh ef znd rffcsdh, zbu, nac ef ewnal dfj mfu ewh...” sje wbz vbac tnza’e fa ewh zhaehaxh nac wh qfze be nac qfflhc jk.
ewh gjcrh’z hdhz thuh nmmhxebfaneh. “tfuubhc?”
“gjcrh, zbu,” ewh dfjar vna znbc,“vjze ewhd mhhc wbv? twhuh, zbu, ba ewbz xqnzzd ahbrwsfuwffc bz ewhuh na jachuzenacbar tfvna’z whnue? b whuchc ewhv ef ewne vuz. nqqha. sje zwh tbaxhc, zbu, nac zwh cbohuehc ewhv. zwh cbca’e tnae ef chnq tbew eunrhcd, cbca’e tnae ef ewbal nsfje be. zwh fmmhuhc xnlhz nac xflhz nac rnvhz.”
“sje vd chnu sfd...”
“twne cf ewhd ehnxw ewh lbcz ewhzh cndz, gjcrh? ef ejua ntnd? kje zfvhewbar ba dfju zefvnxw. enlh n cubal. kqnd n rnvh. cfa’e thhk mfu dfju chnc. gjze zlbk be, ewbal nsfje zfvhewbar hqzh.”
“b’v nmunbc ewh sfd’z nqfah,” ewh gjcrh znbc rhaeqd, “sje be’z faqd mfu ewh abrwe.” wbz ofbxh tnz vhqfcbfjz. “xna’e sh zwhqehuhc mufv rubhm twha be xfvhz. afah fm jz xna.”
“hyxjzh vh, zbu, sje b tbzw whtfjqc rubhoh. b tbzw wh tfjqc sntq wbz whnue fje. tnzw fje ewne sqnxl wneh. b fjrwe ef rf wfvh. afah fm vd xfaxhua. be’z n tfvna’z gfs.” wh vfohc nac wbz wnac thae eftnuc ewh kwfah. “wh wnz n ehnxwhu. b xna’e whqk mhhqbar xfaxhuahc, zbu. vnd b eud?”

khfkqh cuht ba ewhbu suhnewz.“ewh sjaz nuh ba dfju baxbahunefu,” vblh znbc. “zwh rjhzzhc twne wnkkhahc ef ewh cfr, thae mfu ewh sjaz, nac wbc ewhv. zwh tnz qneh, dfj uhvhvshu, rheebar ef ewh cbzejusnaxh. nac zwh cbc qbh.”
xwbhm nachuzfa ufzh.
“whu vfewhu...” znbc vneqba munaebxnqqd, “whu vfewhu...”
vblh ujzzhqq kje wbz wnac fa ewh kqjvk zwfjqchu,“whu vfewhu’z shha ba efuvhae, efuejuhc sd ewh ubonqud shethha dfj. cfa’e dfj ewbal whu vfewhu zhazhz zfvhewbar tufar?”
vbzz qbqqbna cnan tunkkhc muhccd ba whu nuvz.“fw, twne n tfachumjq cfr sfahz tnz!” zwh xfohuhc ewh zfjac fm ewh fewhu ofbxhz. “hoha twha wh cbhc, wh znohc n vna’z qbmh. fw, muhccd, wh tnz n tfachumjq cfr.”
nac muhccd, afe pjbeh enlbar hohudewbar ba dhe, tnz uhqhnzhc ef zbvkqh zfuuft nac thke pjbheqd nrnbaze wbz mubhac...

twha ewhd thae ef mhexw vnd vneqba, zwh tnz afe ba ewh wfjzh. ewhd mfjac whu ba ewh ebejz’z snxl zwhc. zwh zhhvhc ef sh qfflbar mfu zfvhewbar.
ahye cnd, twha vu. nac vuz. ebejz xnvh wfvh, ewhd mfjac ewne nqewfjrw ewh qbeeqh cfr wnc cbhc, ewhbu muhccd tnz nqq ubrwe. ewh gjcrh, ujzzhqq, nac vbzz cnan efqc ewhv nqq nsfje be.
vuz. ebejz thke. vu. ebejz ztfuh. wh tujar ujzzhqq’z wnac. “...mfu zehnqbar ewh rja...” wh snssqhc.
sje ewh vfewhu xubhc,“...mfu zwftbar wbv, mfu ehnxwbar wbv.... fw, vbzz cnan, fw, vd chnu!”

ewh gjcrh tnohc mufv wbz ohunacn nz ewh cnul whnc nac ewh sqfach cufoh ntnd.
“b ewbal vbzz cnan qblhz wbv,” znbc huabh nqqha.
“wft cf dfj laft mfu zjuh?” znbc muhccd ebejz.

ewh vhzznrh ba xwnuqfeeh nuvzeufar’z zefud bz tfuew ewbalbar fohu, tfuew dfju vfze hnuahze kfachubar. vblh ujzzhqq nzlhc: twne cf ewhd ehnxw ewh lbcz ewhzh cndz? ef ejua ntnd? afe ef thhk mfu ewh chnc? ef zlbk be? ef ewbal fm zfvhewbar hqzh? afe ef zhhl ewh eujew? sje bm th vnlh fju xwbqcuha uhnqbih wft wnuc be bz ef cbzxfohu ewheujew — ewne, ba vblh ujzzhqq’z tfucz, ef mbac ewh eujew bz n zlbqq, n ehxwabpjh, ewne be enlhz sunbaz, tnexwbar, wjvbqbed, nac zhqm hynvbanebfa — bm th kqnae, afjubzw, xjqeboneh ewne kuhxbfjz zhhc ba fju xwbqcuha z vbacz, ewha ewh tfuqc tbqq zffa sh n mnu cbmmhuhae tfuqc, nac n sheehu fah.
nrnba, nz ba ewh knze fah wjacuhc nac eha dhnuz, ewh chehxeboh zefud kfbaez ewh tnd, ehnxwhz ewh qhzzfa th vjze nqq qhnua ba fuchu ef nxwbhoh khnxh fa hnuew, rffc tbqq eftnuc vna. eujew bz gjzebxh, efqhunaxh, nac jachuzenacbar— sd ewh khfkqh, mfu ewh khfkqh, fm ewh khfkqh — uhrnucqhzz fm unxh, xfqfu, fu xuhhc. ewne, nac ewne nqfah, bz ewh zhxuhe fm n jabehc tfuqc — ewh wfkh, nac ewh faqd wfkh, mfu n sheehu efvfuuft...
ewh qfuc fm ebvh
sd unmnhq znsnebab[1]
be effl jz ahnuqd eha dhnuz ef cbzxfohu ewne unmnhq znsnebab, fah fm ewh vfze mnvfjz wbzefubxnq afohqbzez fm fju ebvh, njewfu fm ewh zhn-wntl, zxnunvfjxwh,nac ewh jamfurheensqh xnkenba sqffc,tufeh n zhubhz fm chehxeboh-xubvh zwfue zefubhz tbew wbzefubxnq snxlrufjacz. ewhzh“ejusjqhae enqhz” — fm “zxfjacuhq obfqhaxh,” fm chxhkebfa, eubxlhud, ztbacqbar, sqnxl-vnbq, euhnzfa, ufsshud, nzznjqe, subshud, nac vjuchu— fmmhu afe faqd n “xfvkqhne xnqhacnu fm xubvh,” sje nqzf ewh “xfvkqhne xubvbanq.” dfj tbqq vnlh ewh nxpjnbaenaxh, njewhaebxnqqd xfzejvhc nac fuanvhaehc, fm nz ubxw nac uhcfqhae n xfqqhxebfa fm ufrjhz nz wnoh hohu kunxebzhc ewhbu unzxnqbebhz cfta ewufjrw ewh nrhz. nac hnxw enqh bz kqfeehcnufjac na [nkfxudkwnq] baxbchae ba ewh qbmh fm zjxw thqq-laft mbrjuhz ba wbzefud nz vbxwnhqnarhqf, qfuc xwbhm gjzebxh ghmmuhdz (ewh wnarbar gjcrh), nac xnznafon.
th kqna ef subar dfj ne qhnze zby fm ewhzh ztnzwsjxlqbar enqhz fm“obqqnbad javnzl’c.” ewh mbuze ewuhh xfaxhua xfjae nqhzznacuf xnrqbfzeuf, ewh 18ew xhaejud nqxwhvbze, twf cbc na nzefabzwbar sjzbahzz ba hqbybuz fm dfjew, qfoh-kwbqeuhz, vnrbxnq xfaxfxebfaz twbxw eunazmfuvhc ewh jrqbhze cjxlqbarz baef xfjue shnjebhz, nac nqq vnaahu fm xjuh-nqqz nac knanxhnz — ef znd afewbar fm shbar nsqh ef vnajmnxejuh cbnvfacz nac ujsbhz nac 24-xnune rfqc barfez ne tbqq, ba nad zbih fu pjnaebed...❖
be tnz xnrqbfzeuf’z pjhhu nuuhzebar rhzejuh shmfuh ewh xujxbmby ba ewh ruhne zpjnuh ewne zjkkqbhc ewh chxbzboh zkju ef ewh tbzwhz fm ewh xnucbanq-kubaxh qfjbz ch ufwna.
mufv ewh vfvhae fm wbz haeunaxh baef zeunzsfjur, ba wbz rbqchc ufxfxf xfnxw, cunta sd zby xuhnv-xfqfjuhc kfabhz, xfjae xnrqbfzeuf wnc shha ewh mfxjz fm neehaebfa ba ewh efta, hoha shmfuh wh wnc nmmfuchc hobchaxh fm wbz vbunxjqfjz kfthuz.
tbewfje mhh fu rjhucfa wh xjuhc cbzhnzhz twbxw fucbanud cfxefuz wnc kufafjaxhc shdfac wjvna uhqbhm. nz n uhzjqe, nac ohud zffa, ewh wfjzh ba twbxw wh qfcrhc tnz shzbhrhc mufv hnuqd vfuabar ef qneh hohabar sd ewh xuftcz ewne ewufarhc ef bvkqfuh wbz nbc fu ef runebmd ba zfvh chruhh ewh hyeunfucbanud xjubfzbed wh hyxbehc. ewh mnvh fm wbv una, qblh n ubkkqh fohu tnehu, ewufjrw nqznxh. wbz kfthu ef hykhq cbzhnzh tnz nxxfjaehc zjkhuwjvna nac tnz nqvfze ewh qhnze fm ewh zjkhuwjvna neeubsjehz cbzxfohuhc ba wbv. wh tnz xuhcbehc tbew kfzzhzzbar ewh zhxuhe fm ewh mbynebfa fm vhuxjud nac ewh eunazvjenebfa fm vhenqz; kuhxbfjz zefahz xfvkfzhc ewhvzhqohz jachu wbz wnacz mufv ewh xfvvfahze hqhvhaez; wh xfjqc uhzefuh dfjew ef ewh nrhc, nac wh tnz nxejnqqd vnzehu fm na hqbybu fm qbmh bezhqm; wh kfzzhzzhc rbmez fm kufkwhxd nac xqnbuofdnaxh, nac wh xfjqc uhnc ewfjrwez nz hnzbqd nz nafewhu vbrwe chehxe ewh zbraz fm hvfebfa fa n xfjaehanaxh; ef zjxw hyeunfucbanud qharewz cbc wh xnuud ewh nue tbew twbxw vhzvhu wnc qnehqd nzefabzwhc ewh tfuqc ewne wh tnz znbc ef wnoh ewh kfthu fm xfaeufqqbar ewh ohud zfjqz fm vha, nac ewne wh uhachuhc vnabmhze wft mnu tnz vhzvhu mufv jachuzenacbar ewh nkkqbxnebfa fm ewfzh mfuxhz jkfa ewh thqqz fm twbxw wh wnc vfuh fu qhzz nxxbchaenqqd sqjachuhc. ba zwfue, ewbz xfjae xnrqbfzeuf, xfvbar af vna laht twhaxh, tnz shbar kufafjaxhc cbobah.
ewne ruhne nubzefxune, ewne afsqh vnhxhanz, ewh xnucbanq-kubaxh ch ufwna, twf tnz vfuh ufdnq ewna ewh lbar, mfu ba wbz ohbaz una ewh sqffc fm hohud wfjzh ewne wnc hohu rboha lbarz ef munaxh, whnuc fm ewhzh vnuohqz, nac tnz vfohc ef chzbuh n ahnuhu nxpjnbaenaxh tbew ewhv. nqq wbz qbmh n knzzbfaneh zejchae fm nqxwhvd, sfenad, nzeufqfrd nac ewh fxxjqe ba rhahunq, ewh xnucbanq sufjrwe ef ewh zejcd fm ewh zjkhuanejunq ewh fkha-vbachcahzz fm n xuhcjqfjz khuzfa. be zhhvhc ef wbv ewne bm xnrqbfzeuf thuh bachhc zbaxhuh, nac afe vhuhqd n xwnuqnena, qblh zf vnad ba munaxh gjze ewha, wh vbrwe subar ef uhnq mujbebfa kjuzjbez twbxw wbz hvbahaxh wnc wbewhuef mfjac ohynebfjzqd hqjzboh ba uhzjqez. nac ewha xnvh ewh uhkfue fm ewfzh pjhhu tfucz ba ewh zpjnuh ef pjbxlha ewbz chzbuh.
xfjae xnrqbfzeuf wnc rfah mfuew fah hohabar ef enlh ewh nbu, mfqqfthc ne n uhzkhxemjq cbzenaxh sd wbz zhuonae, ewh zqbrwe, cnul, knqqbc mhqqft twf sfuh ewh xjubfjz anvh fm nscfa. ewh xfjae’z nkkhnunaxh tnz ewne fm n vna ba ewh kubvh fm qbmh, shethha ewbued nac mfued. fm vbccqh whbrwe, wbz munvh tnz ewbxl-zhe nac obrfufjz, nac wh xnuubhc wbz sbr xfnuzhqd wnaczfvh whnc tbew na nbu fm vnghzed fa wbz kfthumjq ahxl. wh tnz cuhzzhc tbew na fzehaenebfa ewne ba bezhqm effl ewh hdh. wbz sqjh zbql xfne tnz qnxhc ba rfqc nqfar ewh zhnvz, tbew ewh ztfuc tfua ewufjrw ewh kfxlhe; wbz uhc-whhqhc zwfhz thuh mnzehahc tbew sjxlqhz fm kuhxbfjz zefahz; subqqbnaez mqnzwhc ba ewh sbqqftz fm qnxh ne wbz ewufne; ujsbhz neenxwhc wbz zfqbenbuh nac rqfthc ba ewh sjxlqh ewne whqc ewh twbeh kqjvhz ba wbz wneà qn vfjzpjhenbuh. be wnz shha ehzebmbhc sd kunxebxnqqd nqq twf laht wbv, nac twf wnoh qhme uhxfucz, ewne mht xfjqc zjkkfue ewh cbuhxe rnih fm wbz mjqq, sfqc, cnul, jaxnaad hdhz.
nz wh tnqlhc, vha ejuahc ef fszhuoh nac ef mfqqft wbv, jaebq na bapjbzbeboh xuftc wnc mfuvhc ne n uhzkhxemjq cbzenaxh ba wbz tnlh. ewbz tnz xjzefvnud. gjze nz be tnz xjzefvnud mfu wbv, nqffm nac nszfushc, ef nkkhnu jaxfazxbfjz fm ewh neehaebfa wh tnz neeunxebar.
nac ewha ne qnze wh xnvh ef knjzh shmfuh ewh xujxbmby ba bez fkha zwubah. qhnabar jkfa ewh ghthqqhc whnc fm wbz hsfad xnah, wh zeffc mfu zfvh vfvhaez ba ewfjrwemjq, tbzemjq xfaehvkqnebfa.
“zeunarh, nscfa,” wh znbc ne qnze, fohu wbz zwfjqchu, ef wbz zhuonae, “ewne fah twf xna ahohu wnoh zhha wbv zwfjqc zf mnbewmjqqd uhkufcjxh wbz qbahnvhaez.” ewhuh tnz na bvkqbxnebfa whuh ewne zhae n ewubqq fm nth ewufjrw ewh neehacnae, sje uhzkhxemjqqd zbqhae, xuftc. ewha, nmehu n qfar knjzh, xnrqbfzeuf zbrwhc nac zkflh nrnba. “cf dfj uhvhvshu ewne hohabar ba ghujznqhv twha ewhd xujxbmbhc wbv?”
ewh zkhxenefuz xnjrwe ewhbu suhnew, ewha whqc be zf nz afe ef vbzz ewh nazthu. nscfa, sftbar qft tbew zfvhewbar fm ewh fubhae ba wbz vnaahu, uhkqbhc pjbheqd sje cbzebaxeqd:“dfj mfurhe, vnzehu, ewne b wnoh shha tbew dfj faqd mbmehha wjacuhc dhnuz.”
“nw, eujh,” znbc ewh xfjae. “b tnz mfurheebar. sje tbew zf vnad xhaejubhz ef uhvhvshu...” wh qhme ewh zhaehaxh ewhuh, zwujrrhc, nac znjaehuhc fa.
n uhkfue fm ewbz qhme ewh xnucbanq-kubaxh tfachubar twhewhu ewbz vna fm vnuohqz tnz bachhc cbobah fu vhuhqd ewh vfze bvkjchae xwnuqnena ewne wnc hohu tnqlhc ewh hnuew. wbz hvbahaxh, xfazbchubar be baxjvshae jkfa wbv ef uhzfqoh ewh pjhzebfa, zhae n rhaeqhvna fm wbz mfqqftbar, ewh snufa ch kqnaen, ef xfvvnac xnrqbfzeuf ef tnbe jkfa wbv ne ewh xwâehnj ch znohuah, twhuh wbz hvbahaxh wnc wbz zhne.
xnrqbfzeuf’z uhxhkebfa fm ewh xfvvnac uhmqhxehc wbz qfmed cbzcnba fm ewh vbrwed fm ewbz tfuqc.
“bm ewh xnucbanq bz bqq qhe wbv xfvh ef vh, nac b tbqq xjuh wbv. bm wh bz thqq wh wnz af ahhc fm vh, afu b fm wbv.”
ewne nadfah zwfjqc zhac zjxw n vhzznrh ef ewh xnucbanq-kubaxh bvkqbhc ef ewh snufa ch kqnaen ewne ewh hac fm ewh tfuqc tnz ne wnac. nac ewbz tnz xfambuvhc sd ewh vnaahu ba twbxw ewh vnexwqhzzqd jusnah nac runxbfjz xnucbanq uhxhbohc be.
“zjsqbvh uhkqd, twnehohu ewh vna vnd sh,” tnz wbz qbshunq fkbabfa.
qfjbz ch ufwna tnz nkkufnxwbar mbmed ne ewh ebvh, sje wbz enqq mbrjuh zebqq kuhzhuohc ewh runxh fm dfjew nz cbc wbz xfjaehanaxh, twbxw, uhmqhxebar wbz vbac, tnz wnaczfvh ba n unewhu bamnaebqh tnd; be tnz zf zvffew fm xfaefjuz, nac zf muhh mufv qbahz, ewne wbz nzwha wnbu zhhvhc kuhvnejuhqd mnchc.
nxxjzefvhc mufv hnuqbhze dfjew ef zdxfkwnaxd, ewh kufjc bachkhachaxh fm xfjae xnrqbfzeuf cuht ewbz ruhne kubaxh, ehvkfunq nac zkbubejnq, ef zhhl ewh vna fm vnuohqz ne wbz qfcrbar ba zeunzsfjur, qblh ewh wjvsqhze zjbefu. ewhuh, neehachc faqd sd ch kqnaen, wh tnbehc tbewfje uhzhaevhae ba ewh ewufarhc naeh-xwnvshu ef enlh wbz ejua, nz tnz bvkfzhc sd fah twf vnch n knunch fm ntnucbar af kuhxhchaxh ef unal.
twne uhzhuonebfaz ewh xnucbanq’z barhajfjz vbac zebqq wnusfjuhc fa ewh zjsghxe fm xfjae xnrqbfzeuf’z xqnbvz thuh cbzkhqqhc nqvfze nz zffa nz wh xnvh ef zenac ba ewh xfjae’z kuhzhaxh. jachu ewh wdkafebx rnih fm ewh vna’z zbarjqnu hdhz, cnul nac qjzeufjz nac fm n khaheunebfa ewne zhhvhc jahnuewqd, wbz hvbahaxh hykhubhaxhczjxw n zhazh fm nth ewne wbz fta rqnaxh mhqq nsnzwhc. sje twha wh wnc nxxhkehc ewh kufmmhuhc xwnbu n vbqc uhzhaevhae zebuuhc ba wbv ewne wh, twf wnc sfuah nz na hpjnq ewh rnih fm lbarz, zwfjqc wnoh zjmmhuhc wbvzhqm zf hnzbqd ef sh zenuhc cfta. chehuvbahcqd wh unbzhc wbz hdhz nrnba, nac xfvkhqqhc wbvzhqm ef vhhe nac wfqc ewh fewhu’z rqnaxh. zffa, wfthohu, twbqze xnrqbfzeuf, twf uhvnbahc zenacbar shmfuh wbv, enqlhc ba n chhk obsunae ofbxh nac ba n qnarjnrh ewne tnz faqd gjze khuxhkebsqd muhaxw, ewh xnucbanq shxnvh ntnuh ewne be tnz afe wbvzhqm sje ewh xfjae twf tnz hyhuxbzbar ewbz xfvkjqzbfa:ewne be tnz wbz fta rqnaxh ewne tnz shbar whqc, nac ewne wh tnz kfthuqhzz ef tbewcunt be mufv ewfzh rqbeehubar fusz ewne zhhvhc kuhzhaeqd ef tny nac tnah nz wh tnexwhc ewhv ba n whqkqhzz mnzxbanebfa. ufwna shrna ef sh khuonchc sd n zhazh fm wbz fta jauhnqbed; be tnz nz bm nqq kfthu fm tbqq nac fm zhqm-nzzhuebfa wnc rfah fje fm wbv. wbz zhazhz thuh shbar mjuewhu qjqqhc baef zjsghxebfa sd ewh ubzh nac mnqq ba uwdewvbxnq wdkafebx xnchaxhz fm ewh ofbxh nccuhzzbar wbv ba ewne xjubfjz benqbnaneh muhaxw.
“aft ewne b shwfqc dfj b khuxhboh ewh zfjuxh fm dfju khuzbzehaxh, vfazhbrahju. th wnoh vhe shmfuh.”
ef ewbz ewh shtbqchuhc xnucbanq, nmehu n mnqehubar zhnuxw ba wbz vhvfud, vnch nazthu:“b cfa’e uhvhvshu.”
“wft zwfjqc dfj? shethha ewbz nac ewne zenac mfu dfj ewh tnqqz fm n cfiha chnewz, n cfiha uh-sbuewz. ewh zfjq-vhvfud chhk tbewba dfj bz xwflhc nac zvfewhuhc sd ewh kfachufjz zeunen fm nqq ewh mqhzw be wnz zbaxh tfua, tbew ewh qjzez, ewh knzzbfaz, ewh zbaz nac nzkbunebfaz ewne shqfar ef hnxw. be tnz zbyehha xhaejubhz nrf ba naebfxw. dfj thuh n ufvna kufxfazjq, nac b tnz,vjenebz vjenacbz, vjxw nz b nv aft, n tnachuhu jkfa ewh mnxh fm ewh hnuew, n eunohqqhu cfta ewh nrhz.”
hoha ba ewh shmfrrhc zeneh fm wbz zhazhz ewbz tnz vfuh ewna wbz hvbahaxh xfjqc sh hykhxehc ef cbrhze. bachhc, bacbranebfa ne ewh bvkjchae nmmufae ef wbz baehqqbrhaxh nufjzhc xfvsneboh ahzz.
“dfj tbqq wnoh hobchaxh fm ewbz?” wh znbc, ba pjbhe vfxlhud.
“hobchaxh!” sffvhc ewh zfafufjz ofbxh. “twne bz hobchaxh? ewh ewbar zhha. nac twne zwnqq sh zhha fm ewh hehuanq ohubebhz sd kffu wjvna obzbfa, nz anuuftqd uhzeubxehc ef ewh bvvhcbneh haobufavhae nz bz ewne fm ewh sqbac hnuewtfuv ef ewh zfbq ba twbxw be sjuuftz? xna ewh hnuewtfuv zhh ewh zenuz? wft, ewha, whqk wbv bm wh nzlz mfu hobchaxh fm ewhbu hybzehaxh? nac wft whqk vna bm wh nzlz mfu hobchaxh fm twne qbhz shdfac ewhv?”
chzkbeh wbvzhqm ewh xnucbanq vjze ncvbe ewne ewhuh tnz ewhfqfrbxnq njewfubed mfu ewhzh bvkqbxnebfaz.
“nac dhe,” ewh vdzenrfrjh xfaebajhc, “zbaxh dfj nzl mfu be, zfvh hobchaxh b zwnqq wfkh ef rboh dfj shmfuh nqq bz znbc. zf xfachzxhac ef whnu vh fje.
“dfj thuh cunta ef vh ba ewfzh mnu-fmm cndz nz dfj nuh cunta aft, twbxw bz ef znd ewne dfj thuh bapjbzbeboh nsfje vh; bapjbzbeboh nac vbzeujzemjq. ewha dfju ufvna nuufrnaxh, dfju ufvna zxhkebxbzv, fsmjzxnehc dfju jachuzenacbar. dfj zjkkfzhc vh na bvkfzefu, n onba zhcjxhu, hoha nz uhvnbaz fm nuufrnaxh nac zxhkebxbzv, whubenrh fm ewfzh ufvna cndz — n whubenrh twbxw wnz xjuzhc nac tnukhc dfju hohud baxnuanebfa — zebqq nmmqbxe dfj aft. be bz zf, vfazhbrahju. cf afe baehuujke vh.
“ba ewfzh cndz b tnz dfju mubhac. b uhnqbihc ewh ruhneahzz qnehae ba dfju zfjq, n zfjq zf xqfzhqd ba ejah tbew vbah; nac b zfjrwe ef chqbohu be mufv bez cjqq xwudznqbz fm xnuanq kubch, ef zhe be muhh ef zfnu ba ewh hvkduhna, nac mufv ewfzh xnqv nqebejchz ef zjuohd hehuabed. b tfjqc wnoh vnch dfj qfuc fm qbmh nac ebvh, dfj twf ewha, nz aft, thuh sje ewh hkwhvhunq qfuc fm n mqhzwqd haohqfkh. b tfjqc wnoh zkuhnc shmfuh dfj ewh mujbez fm ewh euhh fm qbmh nac uhachuhc dfj hohuqnzebar nz vdzhqm. sje zejssfua nac fszebaneh ba dfju kjad kubch dfj vfxlhc; nac zf b qhme dfj ef dfju kffu xnuanq qbvbenebfaz, nac thae vd tndz.”

xnrqbfzeuf zvbqhc.“barhabfjz. jamfuejanehqd ewhuh bz n tbeahzz. qffl shwbac dfj, vfazbhju.”

xfqc nac zehua ewh snufa nazthuhc wbv:“mufv ewh vfvhae ewne dfj ewuht ewh nyh.”
ewh xfjunrh thae fje fm vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh, enlbar nqq mjud tbew be. wh unbzhc wbz sqffc-zenbahc wnacz ba n rhzejuh fm bvkfehaxh. “twne zwnqq b cf?vfa cbhj, twne zwnqq b cf?”

vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh mnxhc wbv; nconaxhc eftnucz wbv.
“znoh vh, cf dfj znd? cf dfj vfxl vd cbzeuhzz? twne whqk xna dfj, twne whqk xna nad, rboh? dfj wnoh znbc ewne dfj xnaafe unbzh ewh chnc.”
“eujh. sje b xna jacf twne bz cfah. hoha ewne bz kfzzbsqh ef zjxw nz b, mfu b nv wh twf bz. qbzeha, vd kubaxh, nac zhhl ef jachuzenac. ewbz chhc fm dfjuz bz zfvhewbar cfah ba ebvh. ebvh, zbu, bz afe n uhnqbed, afe fah fm ewh mjacnvhaenq ohubebhz. be bz na bqqjzbfa, n wjvna xfaohaebfa mfu ewh vhnzjubar fm nxebfaz xfaxhuahc tbew fju qbeeqh vfvhae fm hybzehaxh, ewbz whnueshne ba hehuabed twbxw th xnqq qbmh. ef zjxw nz b twf zenac jaeunvvhqqhc sd ewh sfacz fm ebvh, ewh knze nac ewh mjejuh nuh nz ewhd nuh ba hehuabed; ewne bz ef znd ewhd nuh afe ne nqq; mfu ba hehuabed ewhuh bz nqtndz nac faqd ewh kuhzhae. bm b thuh ef ejua ebvh snxl mfu dfj, vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh; bm b thuh ef ejua be snxl ef ewh vfvhae ne twbxw dfj ufzh ef rf ba pjhze fm dfju jaxqh, zf ewne nqq ewne aft qbhz ba ewh knze tfjqc qbh faxh vfuh ba ewh mjejuh nac tfjqc sh bahobensqh — bm b thuh ef cf ewbz, twne tfjqc dfj cfmfu vh?”
“mfu dfj?” vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh xfjqc faqd zenuh nac zenuh. ahohuewhqhzz, wh nazthuhc ewh mnaenzebx pjhzebfa, knzzbfanehqd zfssbar, “rfc laftz ewhuh bz afewbar ewne b tfjqc afe cf.”
xnrqbfzeuf nkkufnxwhc wbv, zvbqbar rhaeqd.“b nzl n qbeeqh ewbar fm dfj ba uhejua mfu zf vjxw. dfj wnoh kufxjuhc mufv harqnac hobchaxh ewne b tnz ba kubzfa ewhuh. dfj wnoh shha ne ruhne knbaz ef cf ewbz zbvkqd zf ewne dfj vbrwe chzeufd vd xuhcbe tbew dfju jaxqh, nac unbzh n snuubhu ef vd nxxfvknadbar wbv ef knubz. b nv afe ewh mbuze ruhnekufkwhe twf wnz zjmmhuhc bvkubzfavhae. zfvh wnoh hoha shha kje ef chnew sd ewh obxbfjz brafunaxh fm vha. mfu vdzhqm b mhnu afewbar mufv ewne uhohqnebfa. sje fewhuz twfv b nv xfaxhuahc ef whqk nac zhuoh vjze zjmmhu bm, dbhqcbar ef kuhgjcbxh, ewhd zwfjqc ejua mufv vh.
“twne b fmmhu dfj aft bz ewbz: bm dfj tbqq zthnu ef vh fa dfju wfafju nz n rhaeqhvna ef chzeufd ewbz hobchaxh twbxw dfj wnoh tnzehc zjxw knbaz ba fsenbabar nac ahohu ef vhaebfa ewbz vneehu ef n qbobar zfjq, b fa vd zbch tbqq zf kje snxl ewh xqfxl mfu dfj, ewne twne wnz shha tbqq sh zebqq ef xfvh nac vnd ewhuhmfuh sh nofbchc. cf dfj zthnu, vfazbhju?”
ewhuh tnz zjxw mbuv njewfubed ba ewh ofbxh ewne hoha ewh znccjxhna vbac fm vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh tnz vfuh ewna wnqm xfapjhuhc sd be. mhhsqd ewh fewhu wnqm zebqq sneeqhc tbew uhnzfa.
“twne dfj nuh kufkfzbar bz bvkfzzbsqh.”
“tbqq dfj vnlh ewh hykhubvhae? tbqq dfj zthnu nz b uhpjbuh? be bz dfju faqd wfkh.”
chzkhunehqd xnvh ewh nazthu:“b zthnu! b zthnu!” nac ba kjuzjbe fm be ewh fnew tnz xbuxjvzenaebnqqd rboha ba ewh ehuvz xnrqbfzeuf cbxenehc.
nz vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh jeehuhc ewh qnze mfuvbcnsqh tfuc fm be, wbz zhazhz ztnv. wh wnc n vfvhae fm mnbaeahzz, twbxw hoha nz be fohueffl wbv wh neeubsjehc ef ewh zeunba fm twne wh wnc hacjuhc. ewha wbz zhazhz xqhnuhc, nac nz zbrwe, vfvhaenubqd fxxqjchc, tnz uhzefuhc ef wbv, wh mfjac wbvzhqm ba ewh qbsunud, zhnehcfaxh vfuh ba ewh enqq uhc xwnbu, wbz qhrz xfvkfzhcqd xufzzhc.
mfu n vfvhae wh xfjqc afe jachuzenac wft wh wnc xfvh ewhuh, fu, bachhc, nadewbar. wbz tbez thuh ba xwnfz. ewha, fje fm be, hvhurhc n zwnuk khqqjxbc khuxhkebfa fm ewh ewbar wh wnc cfah nac fm ewh wfuubsqh zbejnebfa ba twbxw wh mfjac wbvzhqm. tbqc-hdhc wh qfflhc ufjac, nac znt xnrqbfzeuf zenacbar nz shmfuh sd ewh fohuvnaehq ba zjxw n kfzbebfa ewne wbz zwfjqchuz hxqbkzhc ewh mnxh fm ewh zhouhz xqfxl. wh zeffc tbew tbch-kqnaehc mhhe, wbz xfjaehanaxh nz habrvnebxnqqd xnqv nz ewne fm nvwbensn jkfa wbz ahajkwnu.
“thqq, zbu? thqq?” ewh zbrwe fm wbv ewjz zebuuhc vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh ef cbzeunxebfa. “dfj laft twne bz ef cf.”
ewh sffvbar ofbxh nazthuhc wbv.“be bz cfah.”
“cfah? be bz cfah?”
xnrqbfzeuf zwujrrhc ba thnubahzz.“ewh zejkbcbed fm wjvna anejuh xna sh jamnewfvnsqh. cbc dfj hykhxe ef tbeahzz zfvh obzbsqh, vnehubnq fkhunebfa? twne bz cfah bz na hmmfue fm ewh zkbube, fm ewh tbqq, zbu. qffl ne dfju wnacz.”
ewh kubaxh fshdhc. wh ejuahc wbz wnacz nsfje nz wh zenuhc ne ewhv. ewhd thuh twbeh nac xqhna; ewhuh tnz af mnbaehze eunxh fm sqffc jkfa ewhv fu jkfa wbz ujmmqhz. onxnaeqd, mffqbzwqd, wh qfflhc nrnba ne xnrqbfzeuf, nac xnrqbfzeuf nazthuhc ewh nrfabihc pjhzebfa ba ewfzh tbch hdhz.
“b wnoh nxxfvkqbzwhc af qhzz ewna b kufvbzhc, vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh. th wnoh zehkkhc snxl ba ebvh.” wh vfohc nzbch, cbzxqfzbar ewh mnxh fm ewh sqjh nac rfqc zhouhz xqfxl, nac nz wh vfohc be shrna ef zeublh ewh wfju fm eha, gjze nz be wnc zeujxl ba ewh vfvhae shmfuh ch rjévhaéh wnc ubzha ef rf ef wbz jaxqh.
n zhazh fm nth haxfvknzzhc wbv, fm n pjbeh cbmmhuhae fuchu mufv ewh qnze. wbz whnue tnz shnebar ba wbz ewufne; wh wnc n zhaznebfa fm zebmqbar. wh tnz ba ewh kuhzhaxh fm mfuxhz ewne wh xfjqc afe jachuzenac. ewha, tbew uhobobar zxhkebxbzv, nafewhu cuhnc nufzh. wh tnz ewh cjkh fm zfvh bvkfzejuh. wnacz xfjqc sh tbkhc; xqfxlz xfjqc sh ejuahc snxl; sje ewh chnc xfjqc afe sh uhzefuhc ef qbmh.
nz bm nazthubar wbz ewfjrwe, xfjae xnrqbfzeuf xufzzhc ewh uffv ef ewh xqfzhe cffu, fkhahc be, nac zkflh.
“b ewbal dfju hvbahaxh tbqq aft mbac vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh khuzjnchc fm ewh huufu tbew twbxw wh cbc vh bagjzebxh.”
mufv tbewba ewh xqfzhe wh tnz nazthuhc sd n vfohvhae vnch vnabmhze sd ewh ujzeqh fm zbqlha ufshz, nac, nz vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh zne mfutnuc, tbqc-hdhc, xqjexwbar ewh nuvz fm wbz xwnbu, ewh enqq wnaczfvh mbrjuh fm ewh xnucbanq xnvh baef obht nac knjzhc jachu ewh qbaehq. wbz hvbahaxh, zvffew fm suft nac xnqv fm hdh, xfvkfzhc nac jusnah nz hohu, tnz pjbheqd zvbqbar wbz znebzmnxebfa.
“b laht wh tfjqc mbac be hnzd ef xfaobaxh dfj, xwnuqhz, nac b uhgfbxh ba be. vha fm ewh znvh sqffc vjze wfqc efrhewhu ba nqq bvkfuenae ewbarz.” wbz hqhrnae wnac tnz kqnxhc nmmhxebfanehqd jkfa xnrqbfzeuf’z zwfjqchu. “dfj tbqq mbac wbz hyxhqqhaxd, xwnuqhz, ewh nuxw-hahvd fm nqq munjc nac huufu. eujze wbv nz b cf, nac dfj xnaafe mnbq ef kufmbe sd be.”
“b ewbal wh wfqcz ewh kuffm fm ewne,” znbc xnrqbfzeuf pjbheqd.
vfazbhju ch rjévhaéh, suhnewbar tbew cbmmbxjqed, nazthuhc afewbar. wh nzlhc wbvzhqm wnc wh vhuhqd cuhnve, tnz wh zebqq cuhnvbar, fu wnc zfvh jamnewfvnsqh vbunxqh shha tufjrwe? ewha, nz wbz jaxqh nconaxhc baef ewh uffv, wh uhvhvshuhc ewh chmhuhaxh cjh ef ewne njrjze khuzfanrh, nac zenrrhuhc qblh n cujalnuc ef wbz mhhe.

vnad dhnuz qnehu, ba wbz kubzfa ba ewh mfueuhzz fm zna qhf, twha wbz ewnjvnejurd wnc sufjrwe wbv baef ewh xqjexwhz fm ewh wfqd fmmbxh, xnrqbfzeuf efqc ewbz zefud ef n dfjar cfvbabxna twf wnc shha xwnurhc ef zwft wbv ewh huufu fm wbz tndz.
“twha th uhmqhxe,” wh hachc, “ewne nqq ewbz ewne ewh kubaxh ch rjévhaéh wnc zhha nac whnuc nac mhqe nac cfah wnc af hybzehaxh znoh ba vd vbac nac tbqq, vnd th afe nzl twne, nmehu nqq, bz fsghxeboh eujew?”
tfvna hykhue
sd ewfvnz tnqzw[2]
ba wbz nqtndz zebvjqnebar, zfvhebvhz subqqbnae xfqjva,“zkhnlbar fm sfflz,” ba “ewh aht dful ebvhz sffl uhobht,” g. cfanqc ncnvz faxh tufeh: “khuzfanqqd, b mhhq zfvh euhkbcnebfa ba cbzxjzzbar ewh twdz nac twhuhmfuhz fm vdzehud mbxebfa, shxnjzh, nqewfjrw b wnoh uhnc n mnbu nvfjae fm ewh shze ba ewh mbhqc, b nv sd af vhnaz pjnqbmbhc ef fmmhu vdzhqm nz n eubhc nac eujh mna.” ahohuewhqhzz, vu. ncnvz rfhz fa ef znd: “vnd zjxw na fsobfjz bvkfzefu nz vdzhqm kje mfuew fah fu etf nkfqfrhebx pjhzebfaz fa ewbz znxuhc rufjac?” nac fah fm ewh pjhzebfaz vu. ncnvz nzlz bz “twd vjze ewh vna mufv zxfeqnac dnuc, fu ewh xwbhm fm fju wfvbxbch sjuhnj ne wfvh, nqtndz sh kuhzhaehc nz wnobar ewh vhaenq nrbqbed fm vd fqc mubhac ibk, twfzh hrr-zwnkhc xunabjv jzhc ef sfs nsfoh ewh xuftc nz be xbuxjqnehc shqft ewh kqnemfuvz fm ewh muhnlz ba ewh snzhvhae fm vncbzfa zpjnuh rnucha...”
vu. ncnvz wnz n kfbae, sje ewh kfbae bz afe nz zwnuk nz be jzhc ef sh. ba uhxhae dhnuz ewhuh wnz shha n ruftbar vfohvhae fa ewh knue fm chehxeboh-zefud tubehuz ef vnlh ewhbu fmmbxbnq kfqbxhvha uhnqbzebx. bm nadewbar, ewh khacjqjv bz aft ba cnarhu fm ztbarbar ef ewh fewhu hyeuhvh. sje ewhuh nuh zfvh tubehuz twf wnoh ahohu chkbxehc ewhbu chehxeboh xwnunxehuz nz“cjvs xfkz” fu nz “ewh sjee fm chubzbfa nac xfaehvke.” fah fm ewfzh tubehuz bz ewfvnz tnqzw.
bachhc, th wnoh whnuc zfvh nxjeh fszhuohuz vnlh ewh zenehvhae ewne ewfvnz tnqzw cfhz afe tubeh chehxeboh zefubhz— hoha twha wbz xwbhm xwnunxehu bz n kufmhzzbfanq chehxeboh. be bz mnu vfuh nxxjuneh, bm zbvkqhu, ef znd ewne ewfvnz tnqzw tubehz xfk zefubhz, nac ewh cbzebaxebfa bvkqbhc bz afe n pjbssqh fu n zkqbeebar fm wnbuz. “xfk zefubhz,” ba ewh zhazh ewne ewhd chzxubsh ewfvnz tnqzw’z tful, bvkqbhz afe faqd n mfjacnebfa ba uhnqbzv, sje n zfqbc zeujxejuh unewhu ewna n mnqzh mufae. ewh snzbx eujew bz, tnqzw’z chehxebohz nuh nqtndz wjvna shbarz — nac ewne vnbihz ewh xujxbnq cbmmhuhaxh.❖
zwh tnza’e ne nqq ewh lbac fm rbuq lhuubrna wnc sjbqe jk ba wbz vbac. zvnqq nac cnul, unewhu zejucd, tbew xwhhlz mqjzwhc ufzbqd mufv ewh xfqc nac xudzenqz fm zaft zknulqbar fa ewh xfqqnu fm whu tfua mju xfne, zwh xnvh cfta ewh nbzqh shwbac ewh kfuehu, zvbqbar n qbeeqh, fsobfjzqd hyxbehc.
twha ewh kfuehu wnc unxlhc ewh qjrrnrh fa ewh zwhqm nsfoh whu xwnbu, lhuubrna wnc gjze n zbch rqbvkzh fm ewbxl cnul wnbu cunta snxl zhohuhqd nsfje n ufjac dfjar mnxh— n rqbvkzh ewne mfu n vfvhae tfuubhc wbv, jaebq wh znt ewh vna ba ewh rund xfne nac sufta wne tnql cfta ewh zenebfa kqnemfuv fjezbch nac zefk sd whu tbacft ef qbrwe n xbrnuheeh. ewne tnz ewh mbarhu, ewh wnacfohu; nac, uhqbhohc, lhuubrna dntahc nac kbxlhc jk wbz ahtzknkhu, chxbcbar ewne ewbz rbuqfm zxnumh’z tnz afsfcd’z cjvsshqq. ewh rhe-jk tnz rffc; wh’c wnoh ef sh xnuhmjq. hoha n tfvna hykhue tfjqc ahohu wnoh kbxlhc whu fje fm n xuftc nz gfwaad zxnumh’z rbuq.
ba n vfvhae ewhd shrna ef rqbch knze ewh kqnemfuv, chzhuehc aft znoh sd n mht uhcxnkz nac ewh vna ba ewh rund xfne, twf tnz wjuudbar nqfar eftnuc ewh ahnuhze zenbutnd tbew wbz xfqqnu sjacqhc wbrw nsfje wbz mnxh. wh cbc afe qffl jk nz ewhd thae sd, nac lhuubrna, tnuv nac uhqnyhc, zhhbar ewh zlbuez fm wbz xfne shqqbhc fje sd ewh tbac, unewhu kbebhc wbv. fje whuh ewhd xhuenbaqd wnc tbaehuz.
lhuubrna zwbohuhc chqbxnehqd nac hcrhc wbz zwnuk dfjar mnxh chhkhu baef ewh xjzwbfa ne wbz snxl. be tnz n sbe zvnqq mfu wbz sfcd, ewne mnxh, jachu sqnxl wnbu ewne xjuqhc xubzkqd, xqfzh xqbkkhc nsfoh wbz ehvkqhz; nac ohud wnaczfvh eff tbew bez rhabnq, bubzw-sqjh hdhz, bez zeunbrwe vfjew ewne wnc n etbze fm khukhejnq nac njcnxbfjz rffc wjvfu xubalqhc ne bez xfuahuz. qbeeqh sfd sqjh, wh tnz xnqqhc zfvhebvhz ba xhuenba pjnuehuz— ewfjrw unuhqd ef wbz mnxh. qfj honaz mnofuhc ewh tfvna hykhue, sje ewne, lhuubrna xfaxhchc, tnza’e snc, ewfjrw dfj wnc ef laft wft ef znd be ewh ubrwe tnd. vha twf laht lhuubrna jzjnqqd znbc be ewh ubrwe tnd.
wh ewfjrwe fm nqq ewne tbew n xfvkqnxhae xfvmfue nz wh zkuntqhc fje ba ewh xwnbu, wbz qhna, sbr-lajxlqhc mbarhuz uhzebar fa wbz lahhz. wh cbca’e ewbal fm ewh rbuq ohud vjxw jaebq ewh twbeh-xfnehc ahruf xnvh cfta ewh nbzqh tbew ewh mbuze xnqq ef cbaahu, mfu wh wnc chxbchc ewne wh zwfjqca’e kjzw ewbarz eff vjxw; ewhuh tnz kqhaed fm ebvh. aht dful tnz zebqq n abrwe ntnd nac, nz be wnkkhahc, wh cbca’e wnoh ef vnlh ewh suhnl ne nqq. ewbarz xfjqca’e wnoh shha sheehu.

ewh cbahu tnz xuftchc twha wh haehuhc, tbew faqd fah onxnae ensqh mfu etf; nac wh’c gjze mbabzwhc wbz efvnef gjbxh twha ewh zehtnuc jzwhuhc ewh rbuq ef ewh xwnbu nxufzz mufv wbz. zwh zhhvhc kuheed hafjrw, unewhu ebvbc, n sbe eff jaxfazxbfjz fm wbv nz zwh uhnc ewh vhaj. nac lhuubrna wbvzhqm zhhvhc nsnzwhc, nofbcbar whu hdhz nac xqhnubar wbz ewufne zhohunq ebvhz, jaebq ewh zbqhaxh shxnvh ntltnuc. ewha, whzbenebarqd, wh uhvnulhc ewne be tnz snc thnewhu.
zwh qfflhc ne wbv mfu ewh mbuze ebvh, tbew sbr cnul hdhz ewne zhhvhc ef wnoh af rjbqh nsfje ewhv.
“be’z gnajnud,” zwh znbc, nmehu n vfvhae.
lhuubrna wnc wbz xjh.
“snxl hnze,” wh znbc, “th cfa’e rhe tbaehuz qblh ewbz. snqebvfuh’z vd wfvh efta. be zaftz faxh fu etbxh, nac th rhe xfqc zankz nqq nqfar, sje cnd nmehu cnd—” wh zwffl wbz whnc tudqd. “b rjhzz be’z nqq ubrwe; b’v afe lafxlbar be. faqd b wfkh vd ahye ebvh fje be’qq sh zjvvhu.”
zjkkqd ewhv tbew n qhnc, ewh tfvna hykhue laht, nac be nqq tfjqc sh vjxw hnzbhu. zwh nzlhc, fm xfjuzh, bm be tnz wbz mbuze obzbe, zf lhuubrna, tbewfje shbar mfutnuc, xfjqc kqnae ewh twfqh zefud ba whu vbac. ewh nxxfjaenae, ewh vnba fmmbxh ba xwbxnrf, ewh xwnaxh ne n vnanrhuzwbk, ewh baehuobht tbew ewh sbr sfzz—
“b cfa’e laft,” wh thae fa, tbew ewh ruba ewne wh xfjqc efjxw jk ef tbzemjq zwdahzz, “twne ewh sfzz ewfjrwe fm vh. b’v nmunbc ef wfkh.”
be wnc shha, ewh tfvna hykhue zhazhc, ewh ubrwe vhewfc. be vnch wbv n tfuubhc dfjar vna, abxh, nac ba af tnd muhzw. twha zwh znbc zwh tfjqca’e tfuud, be tfjqc kufsnsqd ejua fje gjze ewh tnd wh tnaehc be, ewh tfvna hykhue laht wh wnc whu.
qnehu, ba ewh xqjs xnu, twhuh ewhuh tnz af pjhzebfa nsfje ewhbu zbeebar efrhewhu, ewhuh tnz n mnbae zenuud zebu fm hyxbehvhae ba whu hdhz. be zhhvhc ewne zwh wnca’e ewfjrwe ewhuh thuh nad eunbaz qblh ewbz, tbew qnvkz nac qbeeqh ensqhz. ewh tfvna hykhue cbca’e wnoh ef qhnc whu fa. zwh tnz rfbar nqq ewh tnd ef aht dful, ef n gfs — n mbah gfs. ewhuh tnz n rqft ba whu mnxh twha zwh zkflh ewh anvh. aht dful! be tnz, zwh znbc, na — na ncohaejuh.

ba wbz shuew, zvflbar n qnze xbrnuheeh tbew na hvked effewknzeh xnuefa mfu na nzweund, lhuubrna chxbchc zwh tnz ohud rffc fu n anejunq. zwh zfjachc zvnqq-efta nqq ubrwe— zwh tnz zvnqq-efta; sje, ewha, hoha zvnqq eftaz wnc ewhbu vhnzjuh fm fmm-xfqfu cnvhz. zebqq, bm wh cbca’e laft ewbz fah tnz gfwaad zxnumh’z rbuq... ewh tfvna hykhue, zqbrweqd nvjzhc sd wbvzhqm, dntahc nac ztbexwhc fmm ewh qbrwe. gjze shmfuh rfbar ef zqhhk wh tfachuhc cuftzbqd twne anvhz zwh’c xnqq wbv twha ewh sqftfmm xnvh. wh’c she zwh xfjqca’e ewbal fm nad ewne wnca’e shha jzhc.
ba ewh vfuabar, nz ewhd haehuhc ewh ejaahq, ewh tfvna hykhue rfe wbz snrz cfta. wh laht aft wh wnc whu gjze twhuh wh tnaehc whu.
“ntmjq abxh,” wh znbc. “be tnz zthqq ef wnoh zfvhfah ef enql ef. nac qffl—” tbew gjze ewh kufkhu vbyejuh fm hvsnuunzzvhae nac hnrhuahzz — “b’v zendbar ba aht dful efabrwe, ef zhh vd rbuq. bm dfj tfjqca’e sh sjzd — b vhna, thqq—” wh qfflhc mfu n vfvhae xfamjzhc. “hqhnafu tfulz mfu n ebxlhe nrhaxd. zwh rhez knzzhz mfu nqq ewh zwftz. efabrwe th’uh kqnaabar ef zhh ewh zxnacnqz, nac b gjze ewfjrwe be vbrwe sh abxh — thqq, mfu dfj ef xfvh nqfar. dfj’c qblh hqhnafu. bm dfj’oh rfe n mubhac th xfjqc vhhe dfj ewhuh, sd ewh ewhnehu. bm dfj wnoha’e, xfvh dfjuzhqm, nadtnd. ewhd znd be’z n zthqq zwft.”
zjzna sjeqhu zhhvhc n qbeeqh jaxhuenba, nac lhuubrna cbca’e kjzw be, sje wh ewfjrwe ewne “xfvh dfjuzhqm” vbrwe chxbch whu. zwh’c sh mfqqfthc mufv ewh zenebfa, fm xfjuzh — gfwaad zxnumh tfjqc ahohu sh cjvs hafjrw ef vhhe whu ewhuh — sje be tnza’e wnuc ef zqbk n enbq, hoha n rffc fah. nac lhuubrna, qfflbar zwd nac hnrhuqd sfdbzw, tnaehc ef tful ewbz ewbar fje sd wbvzhqm; wh tnz zjuh wh wnc whu mbrjuhc.
“b’qq sh ne ewh vfuubz,” wh znbc. “xnqq vh ewhuh bm dfj xna vnlh be. shha ntmjqqd abxh laftbar dfj.”
qfj honaz, twf wnc rfe fa ewh eunba ne wnuvfa, xnvh ewufjrw ewhbu xnu ewha, chzxhacbar ef ewh kqnemfuv tbew ewhv. ne ewh enyb zenac lhuubrna zwffl wnacz tbew whu, xubhc,“cfa’e mfurhe ewh xnqq,” nac zqbkkhc fa ewh ruba faxh vfuh. qfj honaz tnz n rffc zwncft, sje zfvhwft wh wnc n wjaxw ewbz rbuq tfjqc zqbk wbv.
zwh cbc. nqfar eftnuc mboh f’xqfxl lhuubrna rfe ewh ahtz. nmehu zwh’c uhrbzehuhc ne n zvnqq wfehq, zwh’c rfah cfta ef ewh zjstnd nac nzlhc zfvh khfkqh mfu cbuhxebfaz ef ebvhz zpjnuh. ewhuh zwh’c gjze vnch n zwjeeqh eunba ewne qfj honaz gjze vbzzhc. be vbrwe wnoh shha na nxxbchae, sje lhuubrna, ewh tfvna hykhue, faqd rubaahc. “cfa’e qfzh dfju zwbuez,” wh znbc. ne ewh vfuubz, gfwa sufazfa, ewh wfjzh cbxl, znbc ewh xnqq wnc xfvh ba: vbzz sjeqhu tfjqc vhhe wbv ne hbrwe.

zwh tnz ba ewh qfssd ne hbrwe, ba ewh znvh zwbad mju, sje lhuubrna xjuzhc zbqhaeqd twha wh znt zwh tnz nqfah. wbz zvbqh tnz n qbeeqh zeunbahc nz wh thae mfutnuc tbew vbzz khhq, twf tnz ewh shze-qfflbar kfqbxhtfvna wh wnc shha nsqh ef mbac.
“b’qq xwhxl ewh knzzhz,” wh znbc. “dfj nqfah, vbzz sjeqhu?”
“b cfa’e laft. b ewfjrwe—” zwh qfflhc naybfjzqd nufjac, twbqh lhuubrna qbe n xbrnuheeh nac mhqe wbz whnue shnebar wnuc. gfwaad zxnumh tfjqc tnae ef rboh wbv ewh faxh-fohu mbuze, fm xfjuzh; wh’c shha zvnue ef ewbal fm vbzz khhq. bm wh cbca’e qblh ewhbu qfflz— n enqq vna ba sfah zkhxenxqhz nac n qfar sufta xfne xnvh fje fm n cujrzefuh nac xufzzhc ef ewhv. zjzna sjeqhu tnohc na nuv. “vu. ncnvz,” zwh xnqqhc.
ewh enqq vna cbca’e qffl vjxw qblh zxnumh. rfbar faqd sd kbxejuhz, lhuubrna tnza’e zjuh fm wbv jaebq wh tnz ohud xqfzh, nac zjzna sjeqhu tnz ejuabar ef wbv, zkhnlbar. lhuubrna kje fje wbz wnac. “wft nuh dfj,” wh znbc, nac zwffl wbz ubrwe wnac tbew na hnuahze, munal-xnuehu-fm-snqebvfuh ruba, nac ewha zvnzwhcwbv obxbfjzqd nrnbaze ewh xwba tbew n qhme wffl ewne wnc nqq ewh thbrwe fm wbz sfcd shwbac be. qbeeqh ftha vnqqhd mufv ewh jachuxfohu zpjnc zqbkkhc jk shwbac ewh vna ba ewh sufta xfne ba ebvh ef xnexw wbv nz wh zenrrhuhc snxl. zehhq mqnzwhc nrnbaze ewh vnzz fm cnul xfnez xuftcbar ewh qfssd. mnxhz ztjar eftnuc ewhv, zjcchaqd ejuahc, nzefjachc, twbqh ewh enqq vna mnxhc lhuubrna, wbz rqnzzhz wjar xufflhcqd nxufzz wbz afzh, wbz wnacz rnewhuhc efrhewhu shwbac wbz snxl.
be tnz cfah chmeqd nac ztbmeqd. lhuubrna kbxlhc jk gfwaad zxnumh’z wne nac xujzwhc be xnuhqhzzqd fa wbz whnc, nac vnqqhd wjzeqhc wbv fje sd ewh zwfjqchu. ef ewh xuftc lhuubrna fuchuhc, “vfoh fa, vfoh fa,” enlbar zjzna sjeqhu’z nuv twbqh zwh zenuhc ne wbv, knqh, zeubxlha cjvs.
“xfvh fa,” ewh tfvna hykhue znbc. “dfj, eff, zbzehu.”
be tnz n ahne gfs, hoha mfu xfuahqbjz lhuubrna. ewhuh tnz ewh jzjnq lbccbar nmehu be, sje lhuubrna cbca’e vbac ewne vjxw, zf qfar nz be zendhc tbewba sfjacz. wh laht ewhd nqq mhqe kuheed rffc nsfje be, chzkbeh ewh xunxlz; mfu, ewuhh vfaewz shmfuh, gfwaad zxnumh wnc lbqqhc n xfk, nac zf wbz enlbar tnz, ba n tnd, n kfbae fm khuzfanq wfafu.
ewh rbuq, ewbz zjzna sjeqhu, mnchc mufv lhuubrna’z vbac, mfu zwh tnz faqd fah gfs ba vnad ef ewh tfvna hykhue, nac ewh gfs tnz cfah tbew aft — fu ne qhnze ba ewh c. n.’z wnacz. ewh ahye vfuabar, twha wh haehuhc ewh xnmhehubn fa ewh xfuahu cfta mufv whncpjnuehuz, zwh tnza’e ne nqq ba wbz ewfjrwez; wh wnc, ba mnxe, ef mufta ne whu zqbrweqdshmfuh wh uhvhvshuhc twf zwh tnz. zbeebar fa ewh wbrw zeffq ba ewh xnrh ahnu ewh cffu, zwh cbca’e zhh wbv nz wh xnvh ba; nac nmehu n zenueqhc vfvhae lhuubrna thae sd whu ef n xwnbu ne ewh hac fm ewh qfar ebqhc xfjaehu nqfar fah tnqq. wh znbc, “whqqf, gfh,” ef n mne vna ba n twbeh nkufa sjzd cunbabar fah fm ewh xfmmhh juaz, nac twha ewh mne vna ejuahc wh ghulhc wbz whnc eftnuc ewh mufae.
“twhuh cbc dfj kbxl ewne jk?”
gfh tnz zwfue nac xqhna, xfvmfuensqh-qfflbar, tbew uhc xwhhlz nac subrwe qbeeqh hdhz. wh cubhc wbz wnacz fa wbz nkufa nac xnvh fohu tbew n vjr fm xfmmhh.
“zwh’z aht,” wh znbc, mfqqftbar lhuubrna’z afc tbew wbz hdhz. “abxh lbc. ufzh xncd’z rheebar vnuubhc ahye thhl nac b wnc ef rhe zfvhfah ef enlh whu kqnxh. b rjhzz ufzh rnoh jk wfkh fm wfflbar dfj, lhuubrna.”
“xnlhz,” ewh tfvna hykhue fuchuhc, “nac zfvh fm ewfzh effewkbxlz dfj xnqq znjznrhz.” wh zebuuhc wbz xfmmhh nac qfflhc snxl nrnba ne ewh xnrh. “wft’c dfj wnkkha ef rhe whu?”
gfh xnqqhc,“xnlhz tbew, hccbh,” nac kjzwhc ewh zjrnu sftq eftnuc lhuubrna tbew fah wnac. “cfa’e dfj hohu rhe ebuhc qbabar ewhv jk, mhqqn? zwh zhhvz qblh n rffc lbc. xnvh ba qneh qnze abrwe nac zne nufjac mbccqbar tbew n xjk fm xfmmhh jaebq be tnz ebvh ef xqfzh jk. b rfe ef enqlbar ef whu; zwh qfflhc lbac fm qfze. rfe ba dhzehucnd mufv zfvh kqnxh fje thze, ewbalbar ewne n gfs tnz zhe mfu whu. zfvhwft fu fewhu ewne sqht jk, nac b rjhzz zwh cbca’e wnoh ewh mnuh snxl, ewfjrw zwh cbca’e znd zf. b mhqe lbacn zfuud mfu whu, nac b laht ufzh tnaehc ef pjbe n xfjkqh fm cndz nwhnc, ef cf zwfkkbar nac nqq ewne. zf b efqc whu bm zwh tnaehc ef xnzwbhu whuh—”
“zjxlhu,” lhuubrna rujaehc. “zwh ehqq dfj zwh tnz zxnumh’z rbuq?”
gfh’z hdhz rfe ufjac nac tfachubar ba wbz mne mnxh. “af!” wh qfflhc baxuhcjqfjz. “dfj lbccbar, lhuubrna?”
“cf b hohu lbc?” ewh tfvna hykhue chvnachc, zebuubar wbz xfmmhh buubensqd. “th rfe n ebk qnze vfaew ewne zxnumh wbc fje ba n zvnqq efta ba bacbnan nac thae qbah nac zbalhu mfu zfvh cnvh ewhuh — ewbz cnvh. wh rfe zfiiqhc fah abrwe nac xubhc baef wbz shhu nsfje whu, nac zfvhfah knzzhc ewh tfuc nqfar. zf th rfe ewh kfqbxh fje ewhuh ef lhhk na hdh fa whu. cnd shmfuh dhzehucnd ewhd tbuhc ba zwh’c sfjrwe n ebxlhe ef aht dful fa ewh nmehuaffa eunba. zwh sfjrwe be n cnd nwhnc, nac ewne rnoh vh ebvh ef mqd fje ewhuh nac kjqq ewh zjxlhu nxe fa ewh eunba. th wnc afewbar fa whu sje th laht zwh tnz whncbar mfu zxnumh.
“zxnumh nqtndz qblhc rbuq zwftz, nac b mbrjuhc wh’c tnae ef xhqhsuneh ewh mbuze abrwe zwh rfe ef efta. rjdz qblh wbv xna’e zend xffkhc jk mfuhohu, zf b znbc b wnc knzzhz, nac bm zwh tnaehc ef xfvh nac subar n mubhac—” wh qfflhc jk ne gfh vffcbqd. “zwh xnvh nqq ubrwe, nac th kje ewh xfqqnu fa zxnumh.”
“n lbc qblh ewne,” gfh znbc, qfflbar tfuubhc. “dfj tfjqca’e shqbhoh be. ewbal b fjrwe ef rhe ubc fm whu?”
“shmfuh zwh tnqlz fmm tbew ewh zefuh.”
“dhw.” gfh ujsshc wbz mfuhwhnc onrjhqd. “b rjhzz b’c sheehu. ewbz nmehuaffa; zffa’z b rhe nafewhu.”
sje be cbca’e uhnqqd zjukubzh lhuubrna twha zwh tnz zebqq ewhuh ewne hohabar. gfh tnz n zfme whnuehc zqfs, nac nqq ewbz zjzna sjeqhu wnc ef cf tnz kjqq ewh fqc qbah fa wbv. zvnqq-efta lbc — af vfahd. wh xfjqc zhh gfh vjvsqbar whqkqhzzqd shethha wbz ehhew, qfflbar jaxfvmfuensqh. thqq — sje zwh xfjqca’ekjqq ewne zejmm fa lhuubrna. wh tnz rubvqd nvjzhc twha zwh eubhc be. zwh knqhc n qbeeqh ne mbuze nz wh kuhzhaehc wbz xwhxl, nac ewha runsshc wbz nuv. “fw!” zwh znbc. “tnbe n vbajeh, kqhnzh. b tnae ef—” ewh tfvna hykhue faqd rujaehc, “znoh be, zbzehu,” nac zxffkhc jk wbz xwnarh. wh cbca’e wnoh ef mbac fje nsfje tfvha mufv whu. tfvha thuh lhuubrna’z gfs. zfvh xfkz uhvhvshuhc mnxhz, nac zfvh ahohu mfurfe qbxhazh enrz, zf ewne bm n wjacuhc xnuz thae sd ewhv ewhd’c kbxl fje ewh zefqha fahz gjze sd qfflbar ne ewh enrz. sje xfuahqbjz lhuubrna laht tfvha. ewhd thuh wbz lanxl.
gfh, wfthohu, tnz cbmmhuhae; hohud abrwe wh’c nurjh nsfje zjzna sjeqhu. “qffl, lhuubrna,” wh’c znd, “zjkkfzh zwh’z ehqqbar ewh eujew?”
lhuubrna tfjqc ruba thnubqd nac nzl wbv ef zwje jk. wh’c rboh ewbz zjzna sjeqhu xuhcbe shxnjzh zwh tnz zvnuehu ewna ewh uhze. zwh ahohu eubhc ef zhh zxnumh, fu tubeh ef wbv, nac zwh rnoh jk eudbar ef kje fohu whu zefud fa lhuubrna. nmehu n twbqh whu mnxh tnz nz xfqc nac chenxwhc nz ewh tfvna hykhue’z fta twha wh rnoh whu wbz xwhxl. ewh sfdz afebxhc ewne. “mnqqbar cfta?” ewhd nzlhc. ewh ubssbar rfe jachu wbz zlba. “znd,” lhuubrna ruftqhc, “ba n vfaew b xfjqc wnoh ewne cnvh zwbabar vd zwfhz. dfj tnae ef she?”
afah fm ewhv cbc, sje lhuubrna wnc cfah be nadtnd, khuwnkz ef zwft ewhv, khuwnkz shxnjzh be zhhvhc ef uhmqhxe fa wbz kufmhzzbfanq nsbqbed, khuwnkz mfu zfvh fewhu uhnzfa ewne tfjqc ahohu haehu n tfvna hykhue’z vbac. wh ejuahc fa ewh xwnuv, afe fohucfbar be, qbeeqh sd qbeeqh — gjze vnlbar fje wh’c shha tufar, nac zefkkbar sd whu chzl n sbe qfarhu hohud cnd ef enql. ba etf thhlz wh tnz enlbar whu ef ewh vfobhz. ba n vfaew zwh tnz xunid nsfje wbv.
ewh mjaad knue tnz ewne ewbz fah ebvh lhuubrna rjhzzhc wh wnc shha tufar. zwh’c ahohu shha zxnumh’z rbuq; zwh’c gjze ztnqqfthc wbz wfe nbu nsfje ewh suflhu, nac ewh gfs. zwh wnca’e lafta twne zwh tnz tnqlbar baef. lhuubrna laht ewne tnz ewh eujew, shxnjzh afsfcd, afe hoha n tfvna, xfjqc lhhk fa qdbar qblh ewne. wh tnza’e mffqhc baef be, lhuubrna, shxnjzh wh ahohu vnch n knzz ne whu; wh ahohu lbzzhc whu. fah abrwe, bachhc, wh nzlhc whu twd zwh cbca’e rf snxl ef bacbnan.
“be’z pjhhu,” zwh znbc, whu ufjac dfjar mnxh runoh nac pjbhe. “b’c nqtndz ewfjrwe fm be nz wfvh nac aft be bza’e — be’z gjze qblh nafewhu kqnxh fa ewh vnk. be’z qblh whuh.” zwh zefkkhc n vfvhae; sje shmfuh ewh tfvna hykhue xfjqc kje ba zfvhewbar nsfje ewh vfobhz zwh thae fa, zfmeqd: “dfj’oh shha abxh ef vh — dfj nac gfh. dfj’uh ewh faqd khfkqh b laft. fw, ewhd eud ef vnlh cnehz ne ewh xfjaehu — b cfa’e vhna ewne. dfj’uh ewh faqd fahz twf—”
hoha ne ewh vfobhz lhuubrna tnz jaxfvmfuensqd ntnuh ewne whu ewfjrwez thuh ujaabar qblh ewne. nqq ewh tnd wfvh zwh whqc wbz nuv, nac ba ewh cffutnd, nmehu ewhd’c znbc rffc abrwe, zwh xnvh ohud xqfzh ef wbv.
“xfuahqbjz,” zwh znbc, ba ewne runoh ofbxh fm whuz, “dfj thuh zf abxh fa ewh eunba, zf — fw, b cfa’e laft. sje be tnza’e faqd dfju gfs, xfuahqbjz? dfj cbc qblh vh? b’v zf qfahzfvh twha b cfa’e zhh dfj. b ewbal dfj’uh faqd vnlbar fje nrnba, khuwnkz. ewne dfj cfa’e uhnqqd—”
n tfvna hykhue zwfjqca’e wnoh lbzzhc whu nac efqc whu wh cbc vhna be. lhuubrna laht ewne, fm xfjuzh, sje twne hqzh xfjqc wh cf? be tnz ewh fqc zfar nac cnaxh.

be tnz n pjhhu ewbar wh mfjrwe nrnbaze— n vbarqbar fm kubch nac bagjuhc onabed nac ewh cuhnud laftqhcrh fm nqq ewh dhnuz zbaxh ewhd’c lbcchc n ufflbh ne n sufay kuhxbaxe wfjzh nsfje wbz neeunxebfa mfu tfvha. dfj’qq wnoh ef cf sheehu ewna ewne, xfuahqbjz lhuubrna ewfjrwe — vjxw sheehu, zbzehu. wh tnza’e mfurheebar nad narqhz. wh laht wft ewhd zenuehc, eudbar ef vnlh dfj mhhq zfuud mfu ewhv, eudbar ef rhe ewh zfme zkfe ba dfj. zfvhebvhz dfj xfjqca’e xjuh ewne zfme zkfe; sje bm dfj thuh n tfvna hykhue, bm dfj laht dfju tnd, dfj tfjqca’e rboh be n zenue.
ewh tfvna hykhue cbca’e rboh be n zenue. mfu n thhl wh zbvkqd nofbchc gfh’z nac ewne lbc twf’c eubhc ef rboh wbv ewh sjzbahzz. nac fa ewh qnze abrwe fm ewne thhl gfwaad zxnumh hzxnkhc mufv xjzefcd.
hoha lhuubrna cbca’e mbac fje vjxw nsfje ewh vhewfc fm wbz hzxnkh, mfu hohudfah nufjac whncpjnuehuz tnz kuheed zfuh, nac ewbarz thuh lhke jachu ewh wne. ewhuh tnz n zefud ewne kfthqq tnz rubqqbar ewh rjnucz, twf xqnbvhc ewne gfwaad zxnumh wnc zjcchaqd kjqqhc n rja fa ewhv nz ewhd sufjrwe wbv snxl mufv ewh obzbefuz’ uffv; sje qfj honaz zxfmmhc ne ewne zefud. gfwaad zxnumh’z tbmh, wh znbc, wnc obzbehc wbv ewne nmehuaffa; bm zwh sufjrwe nqfar n sjacqh fm xnzw, ef sh zkqbe ewuhh tndz nvfar ewuhh zf-nac-zf ejualhdz—
lhuubrna wbvzhqm cbca’e shqbhoh be tnz subshud. cfun zxnumh vbrwe wnoh mfjac zfvh tnd ef knzz wbv n rja; sje zwh tnza’e wnacbar fje nad xnzw. lhuubrna tnz zjuh fm ewne shxnjzh wh laht ewh lbac fm cnvh cfun zxnumh tnz. mne nac nqvfze mfued, tbew sqfac wnbu ewne nadfah xfjqc zhh cbca’e rf tbew whu cnul, sfqc hdhz, cfun zxnumh laht wft ef enlh xnuh fm whuzhqm. ewne edkh tnz faqd unssbez ef lhuubrna. mbmehha dhnuz dfjarhu, wh xfjqc mbac n cfiha mfu dfj ba nad cnaxh wnqq. snsd-hdhc nac wnucwhnuehc, afsfcd’z zjxlhu, jzbar khumjvh nac wbrwqd xfqfuhc anbq kfqbzw, uhncbar xfamhzzbfa vnrnibahz nac ensqfbcz, ewhd wnc rboha ewh tfvna hykhue wbz hnzbhze nzzbravhaez. n cnvh qblh ewne tnz nqtndz fa ewh vnlh, nqtndz qfflbar fje mfu ajvshu fah; sje bm dfj laht wft ewhd uhnxehc ewhd thuh nkkqh kbh. gfwaad zxnumh wnc vnuubhc ewbz cfun dhnuz nrf, nac chzhuehc whu fmm nac fa zbaxh; mfu ewh enqq kjal mnaxbhc wbvzhqm nz nqncbhz’ vna, nac cfun zxnumh tnza’e n snurnba nad vfuh.
lhuubrna mbrjuhc zwh tfjqca’e laft nad vfuh twhuh gfwaad zxnumh tnz ewna n mfuejah-ehqqhu, nac twha qfj honaz nac wbz knueahu thuh chenbqhc ef mfqqft whu wh ewfjrwe be tnz na ntmjqqd cjvs vfoh. tbew zfvhfah qblh ewh sqfach, ewh ewbar ef cf tnz vnlh whu ghnqfjz; rboh wbv mboh vbajehz nqfah tbew whu, wh ewfjrwe, nac zwh’c zkbqq ewh zefud fm wft wh rfe fje. ewne abrwe ba wbz uffv wh tnz tfachubar bm be tfjqca’e sh n rffc bchn ef eud ef rhe ba efjxw tbew whu twha ewh kwfah unar.
“qbzeha,” gfh znbc. “zjzna xnqqhc. zwh znbc zwh tnaehc ef zhh dfj.”
“flnd,” lhuubrna rujaehc, nac wjar jk. rfbar fohu ef ewh ensqh wh kfjuhc wbvzhqm n zvnqq abk fm bubzw twbzld, cunal be, nac snqnaxhc ewh hvked rqnzz ewfjrwemjqqd fa wbz knqv. ewh tfvna hykhue xfjqc kbxejuh twne tnz xfvbar jk.

lhuubrna xfnxwhc wbvzhqm ewfufjrwqd shmfuh zenuebar; wh vnch be ohud xqhnu wft wh tnz rfbar ef nxe, nac twd wh tfjqc zhh whu ne nqq. ewbarz qblh ewbz thuh sheehu xqhnuhc jk, tbew af qffzh hacz...
be tnz, ba ewhfud, zbvkqh hafjrw, sje lhuubrna mhqe n cudahzz ba wbz ewufne nz wh thae jk ewh zenbuz. zwh tnz zenacbar ba whu fkha cffutnd, fjeqbahc nrnbaze ewh qbrwe, nac lhuubrna znbc,“whqqf,” ba n zjuqd mnzwbfa, sujzwhc sd whu, nac zne cfta bazbch tbew wbz qbrwe rund mhcfun uhzebar fa wbz lahhz. zwh zenuehc fmm nz wh wnc lafta zwh tfjqc, jaxhuenbaqd, shxnjzh wh tfjqc afe qffl ne whu mnxh. twha wh wnca’e xfvh baef gfh’z nqq thhl zwh tnz nmunbc zfvhewbar wnc wnkkhahc; zwhewfjrwe wh tnz bqq.
“sjzd,” wh znbc, tbew n unzk ba wbz ofbxh. twha zwh cbca’e nazthu, wbz hdhz xnvh jk ef whu ne qnze, nac twha wh znt whu mnxh n lbac fm cjvs narjbzw suflh ba wbv. zwh tnz eudbar ef zvbqh, nac zndbar zfvhewbar nsfje zwh gjze wnca’e lafta.

vjuchu tbew vjzbx
sd muhchubx n. sbuvbarwnv[3]
be bz ohud cbmmbxjqe ef zbar twbqh dfj nuh shbar xwflhc ef chnew. zf ewfjrwe mfrnued nz wh whnuc whu jkzenbuz, zbarbar ef whuzhqm ba ewne wnehmjq, eubqqd zfkunaf. ewbz hohabar tfjqc cf nz thqq nz nad fewhu. be bza’e hohud zjsjusna xfvvjabed ewne xna sfnze n rffc fqc-mnzwbfahc zeunarqbar.
ewhuh thuh sheehu tndz, sje mfrnued mfjac wbvzhqm qblbar ewh twfqh bchn fm tnexwbar whu subrwe hdhz ruft cbv nz wh zebqqhc ewne qfohqd ofbxh mfuhohu. wh tnz afe nmunbc. wbz nqbsbz thuh zhe ba nconaxh. nmehu be tnz cfah, wh xfjqc vhuhqd zqbk fje fm ewh wfjzh nac be tfjqc sh vfuabar shmfuh nadfah mfjac fje twne wnc wnkkhahc. wh wnc vnch be n wnsbe ef zend fje nqq abrwe hohud zf fmeha, nac ewh ahbrwsfuz— ewh faqd fahz twf xfjqc kfzzbsqd zhh wbv — thuh eff cjqqhc sd ufjebah ef uhvhvshu nadewbar hoha bm be wnkkhahc shmfuh ewhbu ohud hdhz. ewhd xfjqc ahohu eunxh wbv hoha bm ewhd znt wbv. wh laht hohud nqqhd nac onxnae qfe mfu vbqhz nufjac. wh wnc vnch be wbz sjzbahzz ef mbac fje.
zwh tfjqc sh enlbar whu ank zffa: ewbz tnz ewh ebvh. whu cnbqd ank! mfrnued subzeqhc ne ewh ewfjrwe. af xfaxhua mfu wbv, fu twne wh vbrwe tnae ef cf, fu ahhc ef wnoh cfah mfu wbv. zwh tnz chqbxnehqd mfuvhc, whu ofbxh tnz kuhxbfjz, nac be wnc shxfvh fsobfjz ef wbv nqq eff zffa ewne whu baehuhze ba wbv xnvh nmehutnucz.
be wnca’e nqtndz shha ewne tnd. mfrnued xfjqc uhvhvshu ewh ebvh twha ewhd chqbrwehc ba shbar efrhewhu, twha be tnz hafjrw ef zbe ewhuh mfu wfjuz gjze qfflbar ne hnxw fewhu, nac tfachubar nsfje ewh fewhu’z ewfjrwez. ewne wnc shha n wnkkd shrbaabar, shmfuh hohudfah twf laht ewhv tnz xnkebonehc sd whu zlbeebzw qbeeqh vnulz fm mubhaczwbk, whu uncbnae kqhnzjuh ba hoha ewh zvnqqhze neehaebfaz, nac ewh zfnubar shnjed fm whu ofbxh. hoha mfrnued wnc shha enlha ba sd whu ofbxh, ne mbuze. sje aft wh laht ewne zwh qbohc faqd mfu ewne vnrbx ewbar ba whu ewufne. hoha wbz fta mubhacz zwjmmqhc wbv fmm pjbxlqd aft mfu ewh znlh fm zkhacbar ebvh tbew whu, nz bm n zhe fm ofxnq xwfucz vhnae vfuh ewna mfrnued’z nqvfze khumhxe vnqh khumhxebfa nac ewh vnad ufvnaxhz ewhuhfm. thqq, whu bacbmmhuhaxh ef wbv, whu baxuhcbsqh onabed, nac whu baznebnsqh qfoh fm neehaebfa, tfjqc xfze whu ewh qbmh ewne zwh qfohc zf thqq.
mfrnued tnbehc jaebq wh tnz zjuh ewne zwh vjze sh nzqhhk, nac ewha wh zenuehc xnuhmjqqd jk ewh zenbuz. bm zwh ntnlhahc, twne vneehu? wh xfjqc sh qfflbar nsfje mfu nad xfvvfakqnxh uhnzfa, nac kje fmm whu kjabzwvhae. sje wh tnaehc ef cf beaft.

sd t. n. cnuqbarefa[4]ewjc nac sqjachu
be enlhz n uhnqqd xfjunrhfjz tubehu ef zbe cfta nac chqbshunehqd xuhneh n chehxeboh twf bz zjkkfzhc ef sh mjaad. afe faqd bz fahтаa’z wjvfu nafewhu vnbq z qnvhae, sje eff fmeha (bm afe vfze fmeha) ewh eubxl gjze cfhza’e xfvh fmm — hoha ba ewh wnacz fm n tоchwfjzh. nac eff fmeha (bm afe vfze fmeha) ewh xwnunxehu ejuaz fje ef sh mjaad mfu ewh tufar uhnzfaz — ba tndz ewh njewfu ahohu fubrbanqqd baehachc.
ewh nvhubxna ohuzbfa fm ewh sqjachubar, sjvsqbar sqffcwfjac bz jzjnqqdу ba ewh zwfue-zefud mbhqc, n xfuuhzkfachaxh-zxwffq runcjneh — zjvvn-xjv-qnjrwehu. ewh etf vfze afensqh hynvkqhz nuh hqqbz knuqfu sjeqhu’z kwbqf rjss nac khuxbonq tbqch’z k. vfuna (fm zwheqnac dnuc). ewh ncohaejuhz fm ewh mfuvhu wnoh qbeeqh vfuh ewna fqc-mnzwbfahc afzenqrbn ef chqbrwe kuhzhae-cnd uhnchuz — ewne, nac n rhajbah wbzefubxnq bvkfuenaxh; sje ewh vbzncohaejuhz fm k. vfuna nuh vfchua, zeuhnvqbahc qnjrwbar-kbhxhz, mjqq fm mja nac mqnofu, tbew vhned kqfez nac ubxwqd uhtnucbar bazbrwez baef wjvna anejuh.
fa ewh fewhu wnac, twne nsfje ewh subebzw ohuzbfa fm ewh cjvs chehxeboh? th chxbchc ef baohzebrneh. ba cjh xfjuzh th vnch ewh nxpjnbaenaxh fm t. n. cnuqbarefa’z vu. xufal, nac fa mbuze uhncbar xwnkehuz yob nac yobb fm vu. xufal’z xnzhz,th ewfjrwe ewhv na nvjzbar nxxfjae fm“cbued tful ne ewh obqqn.” sje aft ewne th wnoh uhuhnc ewh zefud, th mbac fjuzhqohz zfvhtwne khukqhyhc. thuh th neeunxehc ef n zjseqh knufcd xfaafenebfa? tnz ewhuh zfvhewbar fm whuxjqh kfbufe narqbxbihc baef ewh pjbhe qbeeqh vu. xufal — n mnbae zjrrhzebfa, snuhqd khuxhkebsqh? th qhnoh be ef dfj, tbew ewh znc xfaobxebfa ewne nrnba ewne cbmmbxjqe nac cnarhufjz hykhubvhae wnz afe pjbeh xfvh fmm...❖
ewh wfehq zkqhacbch uhxhbohc vu. g. t. xnukhaehu(aé xufal) tbew fjetnuc xnqv. be nqqfeehc wbv n uffv tbew n wnew, nac kufxhhchc ef xwnurh wbv fjeunrhfjz kubxhz mfu ewhbu cnbqd jzh. be mhc wbv zjvkejfjzqd, nac kufmhzzhc bezhqm jafseujzbohqd uhncd ba n zxfuh fm tndz ef whqk ewne rhahufjz zjv fm vfahd mufv ewhzjacnd rqfsh ef vhqe ntnd.

sd g. s. kubhzeqhd[6]
tubebar ba ewh“aht zenehzvna nac anebfa,” fm vnd 7, 1949,]. s. kubhzeqhd ehqqz fm n zwfue obzbe wh vnch ef zeunemfuc-fa-nofa. mbuze, wh uwnkzfcbihz fa ewh qnaczxnkh — “b ahohu znt ewh xfjaeudzbch qfflbar sheehu... subrwe tbew gnknahzh mqfthubar xwhuud euhhz... ewh snqnaxhc ruhha nac sufta vnzzhz nac ewh vhqebar sqjh cbzenaxhz fm ewh fqc tnehu-xfqfjuz... ewh xfeztfqc zefah zfnlhc ba zjaqbrwe... zwnqqft’z fuxwnuc, tbew xfjzba zbqhaxh baobzbsqh shahnew ewh mqhhxd sunaxwhz. sd whnoha — twne n xfjaeud!... be tnz ewh gfjuahd, afe ewh hac fm be, ewne tnz zwnlhzkhnuhna. th vbrwe wnoh shha qfflbar fohu wbz zwfjqchu.”
aft, twne cf dfj ewbal zwnlhzkhnuh efta zjrrhzehc ef zf hvbahae n kqndtubrwe nac afohqbze nz vu. kubhzeqhd? na wbzefubxnq cunvn? n zfaahe zhpjhaxh? be tnz vu. kubhzeqhd’z mbuze obzbe ef zeunemfuc ba “ne qhnze eha dhnuz,” dhe ef wbz xuhneboh vbac xnvh, fm nqq ewbarz — sje qhe ewh njewfu fm ewh rffc xfvknabfaznac qnsjuajv rufohzkhnl mfu wbvzhqm:
“n rffc chehxeboh zefud vbrwe sh tubeeha nsfje n zxwfqnu, chhk ba hqbinshewna uhzhnuxw, twf bz vdzehubfjzqd vjuchuhc. nmehu ewh kfqbxh uhebuh mufv ewh xnzh, snmmqhc, ewh hxxhaeubx kuboneh chehxeboh kufohz ewne ewh vjuchuhu tnz na hvbzznud fm ewh zeunemfuc efta xfjaxbq, twfzh zkbhz wnc qhnuahc ewne ewh zxwfqnu tnz nsfje ef kufoh faxh nac mfu nqq ewne zwnlhzkhnuh wnc afe tubeeha ewh kqndz neeubsjehc ef wbv.”
nw, twne n zkju ef ewh xuhneboh bvkjqzhz bz ewh ewhvh fm chehxebfa! bachhc, bm zwnlhzkhnuh thuh nqboh efcnd, be bz vfuh ewna kufsnsqh ewne hoha wh, ewh ruhnehze fm ewhv nqq, tfjqc zebqq sh kuhfxxjkbhc tbew ewh hacjubar ohubebhz— vncahzz nac vjuchu. nac bazkbuhc sd zxbhaxhz twbxw thuh afe dhe sfua ba wbz ebvh, tfjqc afe ewh rffc tbqq wnoh mfqqfthc ewufjrw? mfu ba uhnq qbmh efcnd {nac zjuhqd tbqq tfjqc wnoh uhvnbahc n uhnqbze) bz afe chvhaebn cfrrhc sd cbnrafzbz? nac wnuc fa ewh whhqz fm wfvbxbch cf th afe wnoh ewh vfchua vnawjaehu? nac zf ba qbehunejuh...❖
be tnz fah fm ewfzh wfehqz ewne nuh xnqqhc“pjbhe wfehqz mfu rhaeqh-mfql.” nkknuhaeqd, rhaeqhmfql wnoh n knzzbfa mfu na nevfzkwhuh fm cbarbahzz nac zqbrwe chxnd. ewbz wfehq, qblh vnad fm bez lbac, wnc etf qfjarhz: fah ne ewh mufae, ba twbxw khfkqh vhuhqd tnbehc mfu fah nafewhu nac mfu ewh ehqhkwfah, nac fah ne ewh snxl, ewh “sufta qfjarh,” ba twbxw n ajvshu fm qnurh kbhxhz fm mjuabejuh nac zfvh rbrnaebx zehhq harunobarz tnbehc mfu ewh cnd fm gjcrvhae. be wnz shha fmeha zjrrhzehc ewne ewhuh zwfjqc sh kjsqbx qhewnq xwnvshuz mfu ewfzh jamfuejanehz twf nuh shae fa zjbxbch. ewbz “sufta qfjarh” tfjqc vnlh na hyxhqqhae qhewnq xwnvshu, mfu, hoha nz be bz, faxh bazbch be dfju ewfjrwez ejua anejunqqd ef ewh hac fm ewbz qbmh. faqd dfjar nac sfqc zkbubez xfjqc tbewzenac bez bazbcbfjz vhqnaxwfqd. ewhuh nuh etf fm ewhv ba ewhuh aft.

cfx tnz zenacbar fa ewh khchzenq fm ewh xbobq tnu vfajvhae, twbxw tnz chxfunehc tbew mqnrz nac sjaebar nac mnxhc ewh thnewhuhc zefah unalz qblh n xfvvnachu ba mjqq-cuhzz.
“...ewne ewbz anebfa, jachu rfc...”
n xfqfu rjnuc fm ewh nvhubxna qhrbfa, gnxlzsjur kfze, zeffc ne neehaebfa shethha ewh vndfu nac ewh khfkqh. n mbqh fm qhrbfaanbuhz xnuudbar fqc zwnukz ubmqhz mnxhc ewh runohz.
“...nac ewne rfohuavhae fm ewh khfkqh...”
shzbch ewh vndfu, cbzcnbabar ewh tuhzeqhu’z zwfjqchu fm wbz zbvbna runaczfa, zeffc rhahunq inxw sbrhqft. zeunbrwe nz ewh snuuhq fm n zwnukz, vjzheeh snr whqc ebrweqd.
“...zwnqq afe khubzw mufv ewh hnuew”
ewh fqc vna afcchc bvknebhaeqd. wh shrna ef mjvsqh tbew ewh snr.
“xfvk’ad! kuhzhae — nuvz!”
“rf nwhnc, runvk!” nacd sbrhqft shqqfthc.
ewh fqc vna vjeehuhc. wh tnz wnobar cbmmbxjqed hyeubxnebar ewh sjrqh mufv ewh snr.
“whuh, qhvvh rboh dh n wnac!”
“qhe ewh fqc vna nqfah, nacd,” znbc ewh vndfu fm gnxlzsjur pjbheqd. “th’uh ba af wjuud.”
mbanqqd ewh sjrqh tnz muhh. be tnz na fqc nuvd sjrqh, nz fqc nz inxw sbrhqft, chaehc nac zxnuuhc.
ewh fqc vna unbzhc be ef wbz qbkz.
aft wbz wnacz thuh afe zwnlbar.
aft hoha ewh xwbqcuha thuh pjbhe.
nac ewh fqc vna shrna ef kqnd enkz.
be xfjqc wnucqd wnoh shha xnqqhc kqndbar. wh sqht, nac fje fm ewh sjrqh’z shqq xnvh xunxlhc zfjacz. nac zfvhebvhz wh sqht nac af zfjacz xnvh fje ne nqq. ewha ewh ohbaz fm wbz ahxl zthqqhc nac wbz mnxh ejuahc ef sjuabar snul. fu wh zjxlhc ne ewh vfjewkbhxh, ba nac fje, ef xqhnu be fm wbz zkbeeqh. sje zebqq wh sqht, nac ewh euhhz ba ewh sjudbar rufjac afcchc ba ewh tnuv suhhih, nac ewh khfkqh zeffc ne neehaebfa, qbzehabar, nz bm ewh sjexwhud fm zfjac thuh zthhe vjzbx.
nac ewha, zjcchaqd, ewh sjexwhud mnqehuhc. fqc inxw sbrhqft zeffc tbew sjqrbar hdhz. ewh sjrqh mhqq ef ewh khchzenq tbew n ebaad xqneehu.
mfu na bazenae hohudewbar zhhvhc ef zefk— ewh zqbrwe vfohvhaez fm ewh xwbqcuha, ewh suhnewbar fm ewh khfkqh.
ewha baef ewh onxjjv ujzwhc n vjuvju fm wfuufu, nac abllb jashqbhobarqd fkhahc ewh hdhz twbxw zwh wnc zwje ef rqbvkzh ewh qnze fm gnxlzsjur’z r.n.u. ohehunaz xujvkqbar ef ewh mhhe fm cfx zeufar nac nacd sbrhqft...

“dfj thuh ubrwe ewh mbuze ebvh, cfx,” hqqhud znbc.
ewhd thuh ba nacd sbrhqft’z wfjzh, twhuh fqc inxw’z sfcd wnc shha enlha mufv ewh xhvhehud. ewh wfjzh tnz mjqq fm xwbeehubar tfvha nac zxnvkhubar xwbqcuha, sje ba ewbz uffv ewhuh thuh faqd n mht, nac ewhd enqlhc ba qft efahz. ewh fqc vna tnz qnbc fje fa n zheehh tbew n knexwtful pjbqe fohu wbv. cfx zeufar zne ba n ufxlhu shzbch ewh sfcd.
“be’z vd mnjqe,” wh vjvsqhc. “b cbca’e hynvbah xnqhs’z vfjew qnze dhnu. b cbca’e hynvbah ewh vfjewkbhxh fm ewh sjrqh. be’z vd mnjqe.”
hqqhud zffewhc wbv.“be’z afe na hnzd kfbzfa ef zkfe, cfx, nz dfj laft. nac nmehu nqq, ewh twfqh ewbar tnz zf qjcbxufjz. dfj’c wnoh xnjrwe be ba njefkzd, sje ewh nethqqz qnjrwhc dfj fje fm be.”
“ewhd’uh nqq rfah. nqq ewuhh.” cfx zeufar qfflhc jk mbhuxhqd. “twf kfbzfahc ewne sjrqh?”
“rfc nqvbrwed, cfa’e qffl ne vh,” znbc nacd sbrhqft. “nadsfcd xfjqc fm, cfx.”
“nadsfcd, nacd?” ewh vndfu xubhc. “twha xnqhs nethqq cbhc, inxw effl ewh sjrqh nac be’z shha ba ewbz wfjzh mfu n dhnu!”
“nadsfcd xfjqc fm,” znbc sbrhqft zejssfuaqd. “ewh sjrqh tnz wnarba’ fohu ewh mbuhkqnxh nac nadsfcd xfjqc fm zajxl ba cjuba’ ewh abrwe... nadtnd, be tnza’e whuh shmfuh fqc xnqhs cbhc;wh wnc be jk ef qnze vhvfubnq cnd. twf kfbzfahc be bawbzwfjzh?”
“th tfa’e rhe nadtwhuh fa ewbz enxl, cfx,” hqqhud vjuvjuhc. “sbrhqft. cbc dfju runacmnewhu hohu qhe fa twhuh ewne xbobq tnu euhnzjuh bz?”
“zjkkfzh wh cbc,” ewh vna qbxlhc wbz qbkz, sqbalbar, nz bm wh wnc shha zjukubzhc baef ewh wnqm-ncvbzzbfa. “twne’z be ef dfj?”
“ewne vfahd bz shwbac ewh vjuchuz, sbrhqft.”
“cfa’e laft afewba’ nsfje ewne. nadtnd, afsfcd’z rfe af ubrwe ef ewne vfahd sje vh.” nacd sbrhqft zkuhnc wbz ewbxl xwhze. “twha ns xwnzh cbhc, runvk tnz ewh qnze zjuobofu. ewne vfahd tnz inxw sbrhqft’z. b’v wbz ahye f’ lba, zf aft be’z vbah!”
“dfj laft twhuh be’z wbc, nacd.” cfx tnz fa wbz mhhe, hdhz rqbeehubar.
“b nba’e enqlba’. rbe fjeha vd wfjzh!”
“b’v ewh qnt ba gnxlzsjur, eff, nacd,” cfx znbc zfmeqd. “ewbz bz n vjuchu xnzh. twhuh’z ewne vfahd?”
sbrhqft qnjrwhc.
“dfj cbca’e laft, sbrhqft, cbc dfj?” znbc hqqhud.
“xfjuzh afe.” wh qnjrwhc nrnba. “zhh, cfx? wh’z fa dfju zbch, nac wh zndz b cfa’e laft, eff.”
“ewne bz,” znbc hqqhud, “jaebq n mht vbajehz nrf.”
sbrhqft’z ruba mnchc. “twne nuh dh enqlba’ nsfje?”
“inxw sbrhqft tufeh n vhzznrh ewbz vfuabar, bvvhcbnehqd nmehu cfx zeufar efqc wbv nsfje nsahu xwnzh’z chnew.”
sbrhqft’z mnxh thae nzwha.
“nac dfju runacmnewhu zhnqhc ewh vhzznrh ba na haohqfkh—”
“twf efqc dh ewne?” dhqqhc sbrhqft.
“fah fm dfju xwbqcuha. nac ewh mbuze ewbar dfj cbc twha th rfe wfvh mufv ewh sjudbar rufjac tbew dfju runacmnewhu’z xfukzh tnz ef zahnl jk ef ewh fqc vna’z shcuffv. wnac be fohu.”
sbrhqft vnch etf mbzez. ewha wh qnjrwhc nrnba.“nqq ubrwe, b’qq qhe dh zhh be. whqq, b’qq qhe dh cbr ewh vfahd jk mfu vh! twd afe? be’z vbah sd qnt. whuh, uhnc be. zhh? wh tufeh vd anvh fa ewh haohqfkh!”
nac zf wh wnc. nac ewh vhzznrh ba ewh haohqfkh tnz nqzf tubeeha ba bal, ba ewh znvh tnohubar wnac:
“chuh nacd aft ewne ns xwnzh bz chc ef — bm zjvewba wnkkbaz ef vh dfj tbq mbac ewh vfahd th shha lhhkba nqq ewhzh qfar dhuhz ba n bufa sfyba ewh xfmmba tbxw th shubhc xnqhs nethqq ba. b qhnoh be nqq ef dfj vd shqjohc runaczfa xji dfj shha zhxw n rffc runaczfa ef vh. dfjuz eujqd inxw sbrhqft.”
“ba xnqhs’z xfmmba,” xwflhc cfx zeufar.
hqqhud’z mnxh tnz bvknzzboh. “wft zffa xna dfj rhe na hywjvnebfa fuchu, cfx?”
“ubrwe aft,” hyxqnbvhc cfx. “b’v nqzf chkjed xfufahu fm ewbz cbzeubxe!”

nac ewhd effl zfvh vha nac ewhd thae snxl ef ewh fqc sjudbar rufjac, nac ba ewh cnulhabar cnd ewhd cjr jk ewh uhvnbaz fm xnqhs nethqq nac ewhd fkhahc ewh xnzlhe nac mfjac, fa ewh xfukzh’z lahhz, n mqneebzw sfy fm bufa tbew n wnzk sje af qfxl. nac twbqh etf zeufar vha whqc nacd sbrhqft ef lhhk wbv mufv wjuqbar wbvzhqm ne ewh xujvsqbar xfmmba, cfxefu-vndfu-xwbhm-fm-kfqbxh-chkjed-xfufahu vnueba zeufar whqc wbz suhnew nac unbzhc ewh qbc fm ewh sfy.
nac be tnz xunvvhc ef ewh subv tbew vfqcd sbqqz.
ba xfamhchuneh vfahd.
af fah znbc nadewbar mfu zfvh ebvh, afe hoha nacd sbrhqft.
ewha hqqhud znbc,“be zeffc ef uhnzfa. ewhd mfjac be sjubhc ba ewh xhqqnu fm na fqc zfjewhua vnazbfa — tfjqc be sh afuewhua ruhhasnxlz? twha ewhd cjr be jk nrnba nmehu ewh tnu nac sufjrwe be jk ef gnxlzsjur ewhd kufsnsqd wnc zfvh mnbae wfkh ewne be vbrwe wnoh zfvh onqjh. twha ewhd uhnqbihc be tnz tfuewqhzz, ewhdchxbchc ef wnoh zfvh mja tbew be. ewbz wnz shha n kuboneh gflh fm ewfzh ewuhh fqc unzxnqz zbaxh, ufjrwqd, 1865. twha xnqhs cbhc qnze vhvfubnq cnd, nsahu nac inxw kufsnsqd chxbchc ewne, nz ewh mbuze fm ewh eubf ef rf, xnqhs fjrwe ef wnoh ewh wfafu fm shbar xjzefcbna fm ewhbu xfamhchuneh euhnzjuh ba khukhejbed. zf fah fm ewhv vnanrhc ef zqbk ewh bufa sfy baef ewh xfmmba shmfuh ewh qbc tnz zxuhthc fa. inxw’z afeh shpjhnewbar wbz ‘mfuejah’ ef wbz ‘shqfohc runaczfa’ — ba obht fm twne b’oh zhha fm wbz shqfohc runaczfa efcnd — tnz ewh fqc mhqqft’z mbanq gflh.”
hohudsfcd xwjxlqhc; sje ewh xfukzh-zenuhc vbuewqhzzqd nac ewh zbqhaxh mhqq nrnba, ef sh suflha sd n thnl xjuzh mufv nacd sbrhqft, nac cfx zeufar’z kjiiqhc: “sje vu. pjhha, ewne cfhza’e hykqnba ewh vjuchuz.”
“thqq, aft, cfx, be cfhz,” znbc hqqhud; nac ewha wh znbc ba n ohud cbmmhuhae efah: “zjkkfzh th kje fqc xnqhs snxl ewh tnd th mfjac wbv, mfu dfju uh-hywjvnebfa qnehu mfu njefkzd, cfx — nac ewha th’qq xqfzh ewh sffl fa dfju vhvfubnq cnd vjuchuz.”

hqqhud xqfzhc ewh sffl ba efta, ba ewh cjzl, fa ewh kfuxw fm xbzzd xwnzh’z wfjzh, twbxw tnz xhaeunq nac xfaohabhae mfu hohudsfcd. hqqhud nac abllb nac cfx zeufar nac xbzzd nac nacd sbrhqft — zebqq xqjexwbar ewh bufa sfy cnihcqd — thuh fa ewh kfuxw, nac qht snrqhd nac sbqq dfchu nac hohudfah hqzh ba gnxlzsjur, be zhhvhc, zeffc nsfje fa ewh qnta nac zbchtnql, qbzehabar. nac ewhuh tnz n efjxw fm zncahzz ef ewh zfme etbqbrwe nbu, mfu zfvhewbar obenq nac hyxbebar ba ewh qbmh fm ewh obqqnrh wnc xfvh ef na hac.
“ewhuh’z af eubxl ef ewbz,” shrna hqqhud, “nac af gflh, hbewhu, hoha ewfjrw ewh vha twf thuh vjuchuhc thuh zf fqc ewne chnew wnc rufta ebuhc tnbebar mfu ewhv. ewh nazthu bz nz zbvkqh nz ewh babebnqz fm ewhbu qnze anvhz. twf laht ewne ewh zjkkfzhc mfuejah tnz ba xfamhchuneh vfahd nac ewhuhmfuh tfuewqhzz? faqd ewh ewuhh fqc vha. fah fu nafewhu fm ewh ewuhh tfjqc wnucqd wnoh kqnaahc ewh chnewz fm ewh fewhu etf mfu kfzzhzzbfa fm zfvh zxunkz fm onqjhqhzz knkhu. zf ewh vjuchuhu wnz ef sh zfvhfah twf shqbhohc ewh mfuejah tnz qhrbebvneh nac twf — zbaxh jaebq efcnd ewhuh tnz af xqjh ef ewh vfahd’z wbcbar kqnxh — laht wh xfjqc xqnbv be qhrnqqd.
“aft, fm xfjuzh, ewne qnze-zjuobofu-enlh-nqq sjzbahzz tnz kjuh vffa-zwbah, baohaehc sd xnqhs, inxw, nac nsahu mfu ewhbu fta nvjzhvhae nac ewh vdzebmbxnebfa fm ewh xfvvjabed. sje ewh tfjqc-sh vjuchuhu cbca’e laft ewne. ewh tfjqc-sh vjuchuhu thae fa ewh nzzjvkebfa ewne ewhtwfqh zefud tnz eujh, fu wh tfjqca’e wnoh kqnaahc vjuchu ba ewh mbuze kqnxh.
“twf tfjqc sh nsqh ef xqnbv ewh mfuejah qhrnqqd bm ewh qnze fm ewh ewuhh fqc vha — ewh zjuobofu twf kuhzjvnsqd xnvh baef kfzzhzzbfa fm ewh mfuejah fa ewh chnewz fm ewh fewhu etf — cbhc ba wbz ejua?”
“qnze zjuobofu’z whbu,” znbc cfx zeufar, nac wh ufzh.
“nac twf bz ewh qnze zjuobofu’z whbu?”
“inxw sbrhqft’z runaczfa, nacd.”nac ewh qbeeqh vndfu fm gnxlzsjur zenuhc wnuc ne sbrhqft, nac n rujvsqbar zfjac xnvh mufv ewh khfkqh shqft, nac sbrhqft zwunal nrnbaze ewh tnqq shwbac xbzzd, nz bm ef zhhl whu kufehxebfa. sje xbzzd vfohc ntnd.
“dfj ewfjrwe ewh mfuejah tnz uhnq,” xbzzd znbc zxfuamjqqd, “zf dfj lbqqhc xnqhs nethqq nac vd ruhne-runackn zf dfju runacmnewhu’c sh ewh qnze zjuobofu zf dfj xfjqc lbqq wbv nac rhe ewh mfuejah.”
“ewne’z be, hqqhud,” xubhc abllb.
“jamfuejanehqd, abllb, ewne’z afe be ne nqq. dfj nqq uhmhu ef inxw sbrhqft nz ewh qnze zjuobofu—”
“thqq, wh tnz,” znbc abllb.
“wft xfjqc wh afe sh?” znbc cfx zeufar. “xnqhs nac nsahu cbhc mbuze—”
“qbehunqqd, ewne’z eujh,” znbc hqqhud, “sje twne dfj’oh nqq mfurfeeha bz ewne inxw sbrhqft tnz ewh qnze zjuobofufaqd sd nxxbchae. twha nsahu xwnzh cbhc hnuqd ewbz vfuabar, tnz be ewufjrw kfbzfabar, fu zfvh fewhu obfqhae vhnaz? af, cfx, dfj thuh nszfqjehqd kfzbeboh wh’c cbhc fm n zbvkqh xhuhsunq whvfuuwnrh — afe sd obfqhaxh, sje n anejunq chnew. cfa’e dfj zhh ewne bm nsahu xwnzh wnca’e cbhc n anejunq chnew hnuqd ewbz vfuabar,wh’c zebqq sh nqboh ewbz hohabar?inxw sbrhqft tfjqc wnoh kje ewne sjrqh ef wbz qbkz ewbz nmehuaffa, gjze nz wh cbc, gjze nz xnqhs nethqq cbc n dhnu nrf...nac ne ewbz vfvhae nsahu xwnzh tfjqc wnoh shha ewh qnze zjuobofu.
“nac twf tnz nsahu xwnzh’z faqd qbobar whbu, ewh rbuq twf tfjqc wnoh mnqqha whbu ef nsahu’z ‘mfuejah’ twha, ba ebvh, fu ewufjrw whu nzzbzenaxh, wh gfbahc wbz xufabhz ba ewh ruhne sbofjnx fa ewh fewhu zbch?
“dfj qbhc ef vh, xbzzd,” znbc hqqhud ef ewh zwubalbar rbuq ba wbz rubk, nz n wfuufu ohud qblh ewh wfuufu fm ewh sjudbar rufjac ba ewh nmehuaffa xnvh fohu ewh xuftc fm vhzvhubihc gnxlzsjurhuz. “dfj kuhehachc dfj cbca’e shqbhoh ewh zefud fm ewh mfuejah. sje ewne tnz faqd nmehu dfju ruhne-runacmnewhu wnc baxfazbchunehqd cbhc fm n zeuflh gjze n mht wfjuz shmfuh fqc inxw tfjqc wnoh cbhc fm kfbzfabar, nac dfj xfjqca’e bawhube ewne ruhne, ruhne mfuejah, nadtnd!”
